period of more than twenty-four consecutive months, any subsequent utilisation of the property must comply with this By-law and the zoning scheme, with or without departures;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">an appropriate <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) must be made for the alteration or extension of buildings or structures in respect of the non-conforming use;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the owner bears the onus of proving that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-non_conforming_use" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">non-conforming use</span> right exists; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the use right is limited to the area of the building or land in respect of which the proven use right exists.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to subsection (2)(a) and (b), if an existing building that constitutes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-non_conforming_use" id="sec_14__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_3__term_1">non-conforming use</span> is destroyed or damaged to the extent that it is necessary to demolish a substantial part of the building, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_14__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span> may grant permission for the reconstruction of such building subject to conditions.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_15" data-eId="sec_15"><h3>15. Land development requiring approval and other approvals</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may commence, continue, or cause the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commencement" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_1">commencement</span> or continuation of, land development, other than the subdivision or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_2">consolidation</span> of land referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_24" href="#sec_24">section 24</a>, without the approval of the Municipality in terms of subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The owner or his or her <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">agent</span> may apply to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> in terms of this Chapter and Chapter IV for the following in relation to the development of the land concerned:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a rezoning of land;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a permanent departure from the development parameters of the zoning scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a departure granted on a temporary basis to utilise land for a purpose not permitted in terms of the primary rights of the zoning applicable to the land;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a subdivision of land that is not exempted in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_24" href="#sec_24">section 24</a>, including the registration of a servitude or lease agreement;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">consolidation</span> of land that is not exempted in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_24" href="#sec_24">section 24</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">a removal, suspension or amendment of restrictive conditions in respect of a land unit;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">a permission required in terms of the zoning scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">an amendment, deletion or imposition of conditions in respect of an existing approval;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">an extension of the validity period of an approval;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">an approval of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-overlay_zone" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__term_1">overlay zone</span> as contemplated in the zoning scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">an amendment or cancellation of an approved subdivision plan or part thereof, including a general plan or diagram;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_l" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">a permission required in terms of a condition of approval;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_m" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-p">a determination of a zoning;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_n" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">a closure of a public place or part thereof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_o" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_o"><span class="akn-num">(o)</span><span class="akn-p">a consent use contemplated in the zoning scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_p" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_p"><span class="akn-num">(p)</span><span class="akn-p">to disestablish an owner’s association;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_q" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_q"><span class="akn-num">(q)</span><span class="akn-p">to rectify a failure by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_q__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_q__term_1">owners’ association</span> to meet its obligations in respect of the control over or maintenance of services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_r" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_r"><span class="akn-num">(r)</span><span class="akn-p">a permission required for the reconstruction of an existing building that constitutes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-non_conforming_use" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_r__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_r__term_1">non-conforming use</span> that is destroyed or damaged to the extent that it is necessary to demolish a substantial part of the building.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If section 53 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_15__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__term_1">Land Use Planning Act</span> is applicable to the land development, the owner or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_15__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__term_2">agent</span> must also apply for approval of the land development in terms of that Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_15__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_4__term_1">applicant</span> or owner exercises a use right granted in terms of an approval, he or she must comply with the conditions of the approval and the applicable provisions of the zoning scheme.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_5__term_1">Municipality</span> may, subject to subsection (7), on its own initiative rezone land of which it is not the owner for a purpose contemplated in sections <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_13" href="#sec_13">13</a>(3) and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_17" href="#sec_17">17</a>(1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> may, subject to subsection (7), on its own initiative conduct land development or an activity contemplated in subsections (2)(b), (c), (f) to (j) and (l) to (r) in respect of land which is not owned by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_6__term_2">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> on its own initiative acts in terms of subsection (2), (5) or (6)-</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span> is regarded for purposes of this Chapter and Chapter IV as an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_2">applicant</span> and must comply with this Chapter and Chapter IV, including the publication and notice requirements; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the decision must be made by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_16" data-eId="sec_16"><h3>16. Continuation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_16__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__term_1">application</span> after change of ownership</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If land that is the subject of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_1">application</span> is transferred to a new owner, the new owner may continue with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_2">application</span> as the successor in title to the previous owner and the new owner is regarded as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_3">applicant</span> for the purposes of this By-law.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_17" data-eId="sec_17"><h3>17. Rezoning of land</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may, on its own initiative, rezone land of which it is not the owner to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">provide a public <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">service</span> or to provide a public recreational space; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">substitute a zoning scheme or part thereof for a zoning scheme in terms of which the land is not zoned in accordance with the utilisation thereof or existing use rights.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_17__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> who wishes land to be rezoned must submit an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_17__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__term_3">Municipality</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> creates an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-overlay_zone" id="sec_17__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_3__term_2">overlay zone</span> for land it must comply with sections 12 and 13 of the Municipal Systems Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Zoning may be made applicable to a land unit or part thereof and zoning need not follow cadastral boundaries.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to subsection (6), a rezoning approval contemplated in subsection (2) lapses after the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicable_period" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">applicable period</span> reckoned from the date that the approval comes into operation if, within that period—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the zoning is not utilised in accordance with the approval; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the following requirements have not been met:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the approval by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">Municipality</span> of a building plan envisaged for the utilisation of the approved use right; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commencement" id="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">commencement</span> of the construction of the building contemplated in subparagraph (i).</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An approval of a rezoning to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-subdivisional_area" id="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__term_1">subdivisional area</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_20" href="#sec_20">section 20</a>(2) lapses after the applicable period reckoned from the date that the approval comes into operation if, within that period—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a subdivision <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> is not submitted; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the conditions of approval are not complied with.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a subdivision <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">application</span> is submitted in respect of land that is zoned as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-subdivisional_area" id="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__term_2">subdivisional area</span>, the zoning of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-subdivisional_area" id="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__term_3">subdivisional area</span> lapses on the later date of the following dates:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the date on which the subdivision is approved; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the date after the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicable_period" id="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1">applicable period</span> contemplated in subsection (6) including any extended period approved in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_67" href="#sec_67">section 67</a>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The approval of a rezoning to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-subdivisional_area" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__term_1">subdivisional area</span> must include conditions that make provision for at least—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">density requirements;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">main land uses and the extent thereof; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">a detailed phasing plan or a framework including—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">main transport routes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">main land uses;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">bulk infrastructure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">requirements of organs of state;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">public open space requirements; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">physical development constraints.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a rezoning approval lapses, the zoning applicable to the land before the approval of the rezoning applies or, where no zoning existed before the approval of the rezoning, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_9__term_1">Municipality</span> must determine a zoning in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_13" href="#sec_13">section 13</a>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_18" data-eId="sec_18"><h3>18. Departures</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">applicant</span> may apply to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) —</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">for a departure from the development parameters of a zoning or an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-overlay_zone" id="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">overlay zone</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">to utilise land on a temporary basis for a purpose not permitted in terms of the primary rights of the zoning applicable to the land for a period not exceeding five years.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A departure contemplated in subsection (1)(a) lapses after the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicable_period" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">applicable period</span> from the date that the approval comes into operation if, within that period—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the departure is not utilised in accordance with the approval; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the following requirements have not been met:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the approval by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">Municipality</span> of a building plan envisaged for the utilisation of the approved departure; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commencement" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">commencement</span> of the construction of the building contemplated in subparagraph (i).</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may approve a departure contemplated in subsection (1)(b) for a period shorter than five years but, if a shorter period is approved, the period together with any extension approved in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_67" href="#sec_67">section 67</a> may not exceed five years.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A temporary departure contemplated in subsection (1)(b), except for a right to utilise land for a purpose granted on a temporary basis for a specific occasion or event, may not be approved more than once in respect of a particular use on a specific land unit.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A temporary departure contemplated in subsection (1)(b) may include an improvement of land only if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the improvement is temporary in nature; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the land can, without further construction or demolition, revert to its previous lawful use upon the expiry of the use right.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_19" data-eId="sec_19"><h3>19. Consent uses</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_1">applicant</span> may apply to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_2">Municipality</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) for a consent use contemplated in the zoning scheme.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the development parameters for the consent use that is being applied for are not defined in the zoning scheme, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> must determine the development parameters that apply to the consent use in terms of conditions of approval imposed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A consent use may be approved permanently or for a period specified in the conditions of approval imposed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A consent use approved for a specified period must not have the effect of preventing the property from being utilised in the future for the primary uses permitted in terms of the zoning of the land.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A consent use contemplated in subsection (1) lapses after the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicable_period" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">applicable period</span> from the date that the approval comes into operation if, within that period—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the consent use is not utilised in accordance with the approval; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the following requirements have not been met:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the approval by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">Municipality</span> of a building plan envisaged for the utilisation of the approved consent use; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commencement" id="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">commencement</span> of the construction of the building contemplated in subparagraph (i).</span></span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_20" data-eId="sec_20"><h3>20. Subdivision</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may subdivide land without the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) unless the subdivision is exempted in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_24" href="#sec_24">section 24</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1">application</span> for subdivision involving a change of zoning may be considered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span> unless the land concerned is zoned as a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-subdivisional_area" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_3">subdivisional area</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_20__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3__term_1">applicant</span> may submit a subdivision <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_20__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3__term_2">application</span> simultaneously with an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_20__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3__term_3">application</span> for rezoning.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> must impose appropriate conditions in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a> relating to engineering services for an approval of a subdivision.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> approves a subdivision, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__term_2">applicant</span> must submit a general plan or diagram to the Surveyor-General for approval, including proof to the satisfaction of the Surveyor-General of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span>’s decision to approve the subdivision;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the conditions of approval imposed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the approved subdivision plan.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> must issue a certificate to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_20__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_6__term_2">applicant</span> or any other person on his or her written request to confirm that all the conditions of approval contemplated in subsection 21(1)(c) have been met, if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_20__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_6__term_3">applicant</span> has submitted the proof contemplated in that section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_7__term_1">Municipality</span> issues a certificate referred to in subsection (6) in error, the owner is not absolved from complying with the obligations imposed in terms of the conditions.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_21" data-eId="sec_21"><h3>21. Confirmation of subdivision</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A subdivision or part thereof is confirmed and cannot lapse when the following requirements are met within the period contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_22" href="#sec_22">section 22</a>(1):</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">approval by the Surveyor-General of the general plan or diagram contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_20" href="#sec_20">section 20</a>(5);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">completion of the installation of engineering services in accordance with the conditions contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_20" href="#sec_20">section 20</a>(4) and other applicable legislation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">proof to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">Municipality</span> that all the conditions of the approved subdivision that must be complied with before compliance with paragraph (d) have been met in respect of the area shown on the general plan or diagram; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">registration of the transfer of ownership, a certificate of consolidated title or certificate of registered title in terms of the Deeds Registries Act of the land unit shown on the diagram or of at least one new land unit shown on the general plan.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Upon confirmation of a subdivision or part thereof in terms of subsection (1), zonings indicated on an approved subdivision plan are confirmed and cannot lapse.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> must in writing confirm to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_21__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__term_2">applicant</span> or any other person on his or her written request that a subdivision or part of a subdivision is confirmed if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_21__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__term_3">applicant</span> has to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__term_4">Municipality</span> submitted proof of compliance with the requirements referred to in subsection (1)(a) to (d) for the subdivision or part thereof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No building or structure may be constructed on a land unit forming part of an approved subdivision unless the subdivision is confirmed as contemplated in subsection (1) or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> approved the construction before the confirmation of the subdivision.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_22" data-eId="sec_22"><h3>22. Lapsing of subdivision</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An approved subdivision lapses after the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicable_period" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1">applicable period</span> from the date that the approval comes into operation if the requirements contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_21" href="#sec_21">section 21</a>(1)(a) to (d) have not been met within that period.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_22__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> complies with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_21" href="#sec_21">section 21</a>(1)(b) and (c) only in respect of a part of the land reflected on the general plan contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_21" href="#sec_21">section 21</a>(1)(a), the applicant must withdraw the general plan and submit a new general plan to the Surveyor-General for that part of the land.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If an approval of a subdivision or part thereof lapses in terms of subsection (1)—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">amend the zoning map and, where applicable, the register accordingly; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">notify the Surveyor-General accordingly; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the Surveyor-General must endorse the records of the Surveyor­-General’s office to reflect the notification that the subdivision has lapsed.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_23" data-eId="sec_23"><h3>23. Amendment or cancellation of subdivision plan</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) approve the amendment or cancellation of a subdivision plan, including conditions of approval, the general plan or diagram, in relation to land units shown on the general plan or diagram that have not been registered yet in terms of the Deeds Registries Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> approves an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_23__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> in terms of subsection (1), any public place that is no longer required by virtue of the approval must be closed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_26" href="#sec_26">section 26</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> must notify the Surveyor-General of an approval in terms of subsection (1) and the Surveyor-General must endorse the records of the Surveyor-General’s office to reflect the amendment or cancellation of the subdivision.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An amended subdivision approval contemplated in subsection 1 does not extend the validity period of the initial approval of the subdivision as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_22" href="#sec_22">section 22</a>(1).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_24" data-eId="sec_24"><h3>24. Exemption of certain subdivisions and consolidations</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The subdivision or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">consolidation</span> of land does not require the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> in the following cases:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a subdivision or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">consolidation</span> that arises from the implementation of a court ruling;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a subdivision or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">consolidation</span> that arises from an expropriation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a minor amendment to the common boundary between two or more land units if the resulting change in area of any of the land units does not exceed 10 per cent;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">consolidation</span> of a closed public place with an abutting erf;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the construction or alteration of a public or proclaimed street;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the registration of a servitude or lease agreement, for—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision or installation of water pipelines, electricity transmission lines, sewer pipelines, storm water pipes and canals, gas pipelines or oil and petroleum product pipelines by or on behalf of an organ of state or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i__term_1">service</span> provider;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision or installation of telecommunication lines by or on behalf of a licensed telecommunications operator;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the imposition of height restrictions;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">the granting of a right of habitation, private right of way or usufruct; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision of a borehole or water pipelines other than water pipelines on behalf of an organ of state or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_v__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_v__term_1">service</span> provider;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the exclusive utilisation of land for agricultural purposes if the utilisation—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a subdivision, requires approval in terms of legislation regulating the subdivision of agricultural land; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">does not lead to urban expansion; or</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">the establishment of a development scheme as defined in section 1(1) of the Sectional Titles Act, 1986 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1986/95" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1986/95">Act 95 of 1986</a>).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An owner or his or her <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_1">agent</span> must obtain a certificate from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span> that certifies in writing that the subdivision or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_3">consolidation</span> is exempted from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_4">application</span> of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>, and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_20" href="#sec_20">sections 20</a> to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_23" href="#sec_23">23</a> in the case of a subdivision or sections <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">15</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_31" href="#sec_31">31</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_32" href="#sec_32">32</a> in the case of a consolidation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> must indicate on the subdivision plan, or on the diagram in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__term_2">consolidation</span>, that the subdivision or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__term_3">consolidation</span> is exempted from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_24__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__term_4">application</span> of the sections referred to in subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subsections (2) and (3) do not apply in respect of a subdivision or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_1">consolidation</span> contemplated in subsection (1)(a), (b) or (h).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_25" data-eId="sec_25"><h3>25. Ownership of public places and land for municipal <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_25__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__term_1">service</span> infrastructure and amenities</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The ownership of land that is earmarked for a public place as shown on an approved subdivision plan vests in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> upon confirmation of the subdivision or a part thereof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> may in terms of conditions imposed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a> determine that land designated for the provision of municipal service infrastructure and amenities on an approved subdivision plan be transferred to the Municipality upon confirmation of the subdivision or a part thereof.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_26" data-eId="sec_26"><h3>26. Closure of public places</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_26__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may, on its own initiative or on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_26__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_1__term_2">application</span>, permanently close a public place or any part thereof in accordance with Chapter IV.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_26__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_26__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> who requires the closure of a public place, whether permanently or temporarily, must apply in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) to the Municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_26__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If any person lodges a claim against the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> for loss or damage that he or she has allegedly suffered due to wrongdoing on the part of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> when it permanently closed a public place, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__term_3">authorised employee</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">require proof of negligence or any other wrongdoing on the part of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span> which resulted in the loss or damage; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">before any claim is paid or settled, obtain a full technical investigation report in respect of the circumstances that led to the closure of the public place to determine whether or not there has been negligence on the part of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_26__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may pay a claim if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the circumstances of the loss or damage reveal that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span> acted wrongfully;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of loss of or damage to property, the claimant has proved his or her loss or damage;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of personal injury, the claimant has provided proof of a fair and reasonable quantum;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">no claim has been paid by personal insurance covering the same loss; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">any relevant information as requested by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__term_1">authorised employee</span> has been received.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_26__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The ownership of the land comprising any public place, or a part thereof, that is permanently closed in terms of this section continues to vest in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_5__term_1">Municipality</span> unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_5__term_2">Municipality</span> determines otherwise.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_26__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__term_1">Municipal Manager</span> may, without complying with Chapter IV, temporarily close a public place—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">for the purpose of, or pending, the construction, reconstruction or maintenance of the public place;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">for the purpose of, or pending, the construction, extension, maintenance or demolition of any building, structure, works or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1">service</span> alongside, on, across, through, over or under the public place;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if the public place is in a state that is dangerous to the public;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">by reason of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_d__term_1">emergency</span> or public event that requires special measures for the control of traffic or crowds; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_6__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">for any other reason that renders the temporary closing of the public place necessary or desirable.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_26__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__subsec_7__term_1">Municipality</span> must notify the Surveyor-General of an approval in terms of subsection (1) and the Surveyor-General must endorse the records of the Surveyor-General’s office to reflect the closure of the public place.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_27" data-eId="sec_27"><h3>27. Services arising from subdivision</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subsequent to the approval of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">application</span> for subdivision in terms of this By-law, the owner of any land unit originating from the subdivision must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">allow that the following be conveyed across his or her land unit as may be reasonably required in respect of other land units originating from the subdivision:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">gas mains;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">electricity cables;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">telephone cables;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">television cables;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">other electronic infrastructure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">main and other water pipes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">foul sewers;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_viii" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_viii"><span class="akn-num">(viii)</span><span class="akn-p">storm-water pipes; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ix" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ix"><span class="akn-num">(ix)</span><span class="akn-p">ditches and channels;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">allow the following on his or her land unit if considered necessary and in the manner and position as may be reasonably required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span>:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">surface installations such as mini-substations;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">meter kiosks; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii__term_1">service</span> pillars;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">allow access to the land unit at any reasonable time for the purpose of constructing, altering, removing or inspecting any works referred to in paragraph (a) or (b); and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">receive material or permit excavation on the land unit as may be required to allow use of the full width of an abutting street and to provide a safe and proper slope to its bank where necessitated by differences between the level of the street as finally constructed and the level of the land unit unless he or she elects to build retaining walls to the satisfaction of and within a period to be determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_28" data-eId="sec_28"><h3>28. Certification by <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_28__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__term_1">Municipality</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person may apply to the Registrar of Deeds to register the transfer of a land unit, a certificate of title or certificate of consolidated title, as the case may be, in any of the instances referred to in subsection (3)(a) to (d) only if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> has issued a certificate in terms of this section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Registrar of Deeds may register the transfer of a land unit, a certificate of title or certificate of consolidated title, as the case may be, in any of the instances referred to in subsection (3)(a) to (d) only if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> has issued a certificate in terms of this section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must issue a certificate to transfer a land unit contemplated in subsections (1) and (2) if the owner provides the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> with the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">where an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">owners’ association</span> has been established in respect of that land unit, a conveyancer’s certificate confirming that money due by the transferor of the land unit to that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2">owners’ association</span> has been paid, or that provision has been made to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_3"
