data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_3">owners’ association</span> for the payment thereof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of any existing contravention penalty due by the transferor of the land unit, proof of payment of the penalty or proof of compliance with an instruction in a compliance notice issued to the transferor in terms of Chapter IX;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in the case of the first registration of the transfer of ownership of a land unit arising from a subdivision to any person other than the developer and where an owner’s association is constituted, proof that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">all common property arising from the subdivision has been transferred to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">owners’ association</span> by virtue of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_29" href="#sec_29">section 29</a>(3)(e); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">all common property arising from the subdivision will be transferred to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1">owners’ association</span> simultaneously with the registration of the transfer of that land unit;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in the case of the first registration of the transfer of ownership, a certificate of consolidated title or certificate of registered title of a land unit arising from a subdivision and that leads to the confirmation of the subdivision, proof that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">land needed for public purposes or other municipal infrastructure as contemplated in terms of a condition imposed under <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a> has been transferred to the Municipality or will be transferred to the Municipality simultaneously with the registration of the transfer of that land unit, certificate of consolidated title or certificate of registered title;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the engineering services and amenities that must be provided in connection with the subdivision are available; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a certificate contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_20" href="#sec_20">section 20</a>(6) has been issued by the Municipality.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_29" data-eId="sec_29"><h3>29. Owners’ associations</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_29__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may, when approving an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_29__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> for a subdivision of land, impose conditions relating to the compulsory establishment of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_1__term_3">owners’ association</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_29__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_1__term_4">applicant</span> for an area determined in the conditions.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_2__term_1">owners’ association</span> that comes into being by virtue of subsection (1) is a juristic person and must have a constitution.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The constitution of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">owners’ association</span> must be approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> before registration of the transfer of the first land unit and must make provision for—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">owners’ association</span> to formally represent the collective mutual interests of the area, suburb or neighbourhood set out in the constitution in accordance with the conditions of approval;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">control over and maintenance of buildings, services or amenities arising from the subdivision;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the regulation of at least one annual meeting with its members;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">control over the design guidelines of the buildings and erven arising from the subdivision;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the ownership by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1">owners’ association</span> of all common property arising from the subdivision, including—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">private open spaces;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">private roads; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">land required for services provided by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_1">owners’ association</span>;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">enforcement of conditions of approval or management plans;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">procedures to obtain the consent of the members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__term_1">owners’ association</span> to transfer an erf in the event that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__term_2">owners’ association</span> ceases to function; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">the implementation and enforcement by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_3__list_1__item_h__term_1">owners’ association</span> of the provisions of the constitution.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The constitution of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_4__term_1">owners’ association</span> may have other objectives as set by the association but may not contain provisions that are in conflict with any law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The constitution of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_5__term_1">owners’ association</span> takes effect upon the registration of the transfer of ownership of the first land unit to a person other than the developer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_6__term_1">owners’ association</span> may amend its constitution when necessary, but if an amendment affects the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_29__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_6__term_2">Municipality</span> or a provision referred to in subsection (3), the amendment must also be approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_29__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_6__term_3">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">owners’ association</span> that comes into being by virtue of subsection (1) —</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">has as its members all the owners of the land units arising from the subdivision and their successors in title, who are jointly liable for expenditure incurred in connection with the association; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is upon registration of the transfer of ownership of the first land unit to a person other than the developer automatically established.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_29__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_29__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The design guidelines contemplated in subsection (3)(d) may introduce more restrictive development rules than the rules provided for in the zoning scheme.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_30" data-eId="sec_30"><h3>30. Owners’ associations that cease to function</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owners’ association</span> ceases to function or carry out its obligations any affected person, including a member of the association, may apply—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(p) to disestablish the owners’ association subject to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the amendment of the conditions of approval to remove the obligation to establish an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">owners’ association</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the amendment of title conditions pertaining to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1">owners’ association</span>, to remove any obligation in respect of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2">owners’ association</span>;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(q) for appropriate action by the Municipality to rectify a failure of the owners’ association to meet any of its obligations in respect of the control over or maintenance of services contemplated in subsection 29(3)(b); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to the High Court to appoint an administrator who must exercise the powers of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">owners’ association</span> to the exclusion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">owners’ association</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In considering an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">application</span> contemplated in subsection (1)(a), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> must have regard to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the purpose of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">owners’ association</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">who will take over the control over and maintenance of services for which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">owners’ association</span> is responsible; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the impact of the disestablishment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">owners’ association</span> on the members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">owners’ association</span> and the community concerned.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> or the affected person may recover from the members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_30__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_3__term_2">owners’ association</span> the amount of any expenditure incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_3__term_3">Municipality</span> or that affected person, as the case may be, in respect of any action taken in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The amount of any expenditure so recovered is, for the purposes of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_29" href="#sec_29">section 29</a>(7)(a), considered to be expenditure incurred in connection with the owners’ association.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_31" data-eId="sec_31"><h3>31. Consolidation of land units</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may consolidate land without the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) unless the consolidation is exempted in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_24" href="#sec_24">section 24</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> approves a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">consolidation</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">applicant</span> must submit a diagram to the Surveyor-General for approval, including proof to the satisfaction of the Surveyor-General of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span>’s decision to approve the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">consolidation</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the conditions of approval imposed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">consolidation</span> plan.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> approves a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_2">consolidation</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_3">Municipality</span> must amend the zoning map and, where applicable, the register, accordingly.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_32" data-eId="sec_32"><h3>32. Lapsing of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_32__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__term_1">consolidation</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_32__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__term_1">consolidation</span> of land units lapses if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_32__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__term_2">consolidation</span> is not registered in terms of the Deeds Registries Act within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicable_period" id="sec_32__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__term_3">applicable period</span> from the date that the approval comes into operation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If an approval of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">consolidation</span> lapses in terms of subsection (1)—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">amend the zoning map, and where applicable the register, accordingly; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">notify the Surveyor-General accordingly; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the Surveyor-General must endorse the records of the Surveyor­-General’s office to reflect the notification that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">consolidation</span> has lapsed.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_33" data-eId="sec_33"><h3>33. Removal, suspension or amendment of restrictive conditions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">remove or amend a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">restrictive condition</span> permanently;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">suspend or amend a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">restrictive condition</span> for a period specified in the approval; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">remove, suspend or amend a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">restrictive condition</span> as contemplated in paragraph (a) or (b) subject to conditions of approval.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When an owner applies for a removal, suspension or amendment of restrictive conditions, the owner must in addition to the procedures set out in Chapter IV—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">submit a certified copy of the relevant title deed to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if there is a mortgage bond registered in respect of the land concerned, submit the bondholder’s consent to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must cause a notice of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">application</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(f) to be served on—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">all organs of state that may have an interest in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">restrictive condition</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a person whose rights or legitimate expectations will be affected by the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">all persons mentioned in the title deed for whose benefit the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">restrictive condition</span> applies.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> considers the removal, suspension or amendment of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_2">restrictive condition</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_3">Municipality</span> must have regard to the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the financial or other value of the rights in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">restrictive condition</span> enjoyed by a person or entity, irrespective of whether these rights are personal or vest in the person as the owner of a dominant tenement;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the personal benefits which accrue to the holder of rights in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">restrictive condition</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the personal benefits which will accrue to the person seeking the removal, suspension or amendment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">restrictive condition</span> if it is amended, suspended or removed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the social benefit of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1">restrictive condition</span> remaining in place in its existing form;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the social benefit of the removal, suspension or amendment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__term_1">restrictive condition</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">whether the removal, suspension or amendment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_f__term_1">restrictive condition</span> will completely remove all rights enjoyed by the beneficiary or only some of those rights.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An approval to remove, suspend or amend a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">restrictive condition</span> comes into operation—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if no appeal has been lodged, after the expiry of the period contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_79" href="#sec_79">section 79</a>(2) within which an appeal must be lodged; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if an appeal has been lodged, when the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> has decided on the appeal.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> must cause a notice of the decision to remove, suspend or amend a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__term_2">restrictive condition</span> to be published in the <i>Provincial Gazette</i> after the decision comes into operation as contemplated in subsection (5) and notify the Registrar of Deeds of the decision.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an owner intends to apply in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2) for land development that is contrary to a restrictive condition applicable to the land concerned, the owner must when the application for land development is submitted simultaneously apply for the removal, suspension or amendment of the restrictive condition.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_8__term_1">Municipality</span> must consider the land development <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_33__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_8__term_2">application</span> and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_33__subsec_8__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_8__term_3">application</span> for the removal, suspension or amendment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_33__subsec_8__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_8__term_4">restrictive condition</span> contemplated in subsection (7) together and make an integrated decision.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_34" data-eId="sec_34"><h3>34. Endorsements in connection with removal, suspension or amendment of restrictive conditions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1">applicant</span> at whose instance a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2">restrictive condition</span> is removed, suspended or amended must, after the publication of a notice contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_33" href="#sec_33">section 33</a>(6) in the <i>Provincial Gazette</i>, apply to the Registrar of Deeds to make the appropriate entries in, and endorsements on, any relevant register or title deed to reflect the removal, suspension or amendment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_3">restrictive condition</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The Registrar of Deeds may require proof of the removal, suspension or amendment of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">restrictive condition</span> from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">applicant</span>, including the submission of the following to the Registrar of Deeds:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a copy of the approval;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the original title deed; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a copy of the notice contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_33" href="#sec_33">section 33</a>(6) as published in the <i>Provincial Gazette</i>.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_IV" data-eId="chp_IV"><h2>Chapter IV<br>Application procedures</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_35" data-eId="sec_35"><h3>35. Manner and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_35__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__term_1">date of notification</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any serving of a notice or notification or acknowledgement given in terms of this By-law must be in writing and may be issued to a person—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">by delivering it by hand to the person;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">by sending it by registered mail—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">to that person’s business or residential address and municipal billing address, where the billing address differs from the business or residential address; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a juristic person, to its registered address or principal place of business and municipal billing address, where the billing address differs from the business or residential address;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">by means of data messages contemplated in the Electronic Communications and Transactions Act, 2002 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2002/25" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2002/25">Act 25 of 2002</a>), by sending a copy of the notice to the person, if the person has an email address or other electronic address; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">where an address is unknown despite reasonable enquiry, by publishing it once in the <i>Provincial Gazette</i> and once in a local newspaper circulating in the area of that person’s last known residential or business address.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">date of notification</span> in respect of a notice served or given to a person in terms of this By-law—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if it was served by certified or registered post, is the date of registration of the notice;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if it was delivered to that person personally, is the date of delivery to that person;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if it was left at that person’s place of residence, work or business in the Republic with a person apparently over the age of sixteen years, is the date on which it was left with that person;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if it was displayed in a conspicuous place on the property or premises to which it pertains, is the date that it is posted on that place; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">it was e-mailed or sent to an electronic address, is the date that it was received by that person as contemplated in the Electronic Communications and Transactions Act, 2002.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may determine specific methods of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">service</span> and notification in respect of applications and appeals, including—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">information specifications relating to matters such as size, scale, colour, hard copy, number of copies, electronic format and file format;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the manner of submission to and communication with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the method by which a person may be notified;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">other information requirements; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">other procedural requirements.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_36" data-eId="sec_36"><h3>36. Procedures for applications</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_1">applicant</span> must comply with the procedures in this Chapter and, where applicable, the specific procedures provided for in Chapter III of this By­-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_36__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> may apply simultaneously for different types of applications for land development in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_37" data-eId="sec_37"><h3>37. Pre-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_37__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__term_1">application</span> consultation</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require an owner who intends to submit an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> or his or her <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_3">agent</span> to meet with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_4">authorised employee</span> and, where applicable, with employees of other relevant organs of state for a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pre_application_consultation" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_5">pre-application consultation</span> before he or she submits an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_6">application</span> to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_7">Municipality</span> in order to determine the information and documents that must be submitted with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_8">application</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may issue guidelines regarding—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">applications that require a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pre_application_consultation" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">pre-application consultation</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the nature of the information and documents that must be submitted with an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the attendance of employees from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">Municipality</span> or other organs of state at a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pre_application_consultation" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">pre-application consultation</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the procedures at a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pre_application_consultation" id="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">pre-application consultation</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_37__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> must keep minutes of the proceedings of a pre­-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_37__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3__term_2">application</span> consultation.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_38" data-eId="sec_38"><h3>38. Information required</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_38__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to subsection (2), an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">application</span> must be accompanied by the following information and documents where applicable:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> form provided by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">Municipality</span>, completed and signed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">applicant</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">applicant</span> is an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">agent</span>, a power of attorney authorising the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">applicant</span> to make the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4">application</span> on behalf of the owner;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if the owner of the land is a company, closed corporation, trust, body corporate or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">owners’ association</span>, proof that the person is authorised to make the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">application</span> on behalf of the company, closed corporation, trust, body corporate or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3">owners’ association</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">proof of registered ownership or any other relevant right held in the land concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">if a mortgage bond is registered in respect of the land concerned, the bondholder’s consent;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">a written motivation for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">application</span> based on the applicable criteria referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_65" href="#sec_65">section 65</a>, excluding <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_65" href="#sec_65">sections 65</a>(a), (b), (d), (e) and (g);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">a copy of the Surveyor-General’s diagram of the property concerned or, if it does not exist, an extract from the relevant general plan;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">a locality plan and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1">site development plan</span>, if required, or a plan showing the proposed land development in its cadastral context;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in the case of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__term_1">application</span> for the subdivision of land, copies of the subdivision plan showing the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the location of the proposed land units;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the proposed zonings in respect of the proposed land units;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">all existing structures on the property and abutting properties;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">the proposed public places and the land needed for public purposes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">the existing access points;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">all servitudes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">contours with at least a one-meter interval or such other interval as may be approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_vii__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_vii__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_viii" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_viii"><span class="akn-num">(viii)</span><span class="akn-p">the street furniture;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_ix" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_ix"><span class="akn-num">(ix)</span><span class="akn-p">the lamp, electricity and telephone posts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_x" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_x"><span class="akn-num">(x)</span><span class="akn-p">the electricity transformers and mini-substations;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xi" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xi"><span class="akn-num">(xi)</span><span class="akn-p">the storm-water channels and catchpits;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xii" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xii"><span class="akn-num">(xii)</span><span class="akn-p">the sewerage lines and connection points;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xiii" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xiii"><span class="akn-num">(xiii)</span><span class="akn-p">any significant natural features; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xiv" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_xiv"><span class="akn-num">(xiv)</span><span class="akn-p">all distances and areas to scale;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">proof of an agreement or permission if the proposed land development requires a servitude over land or access to a provincial or national road;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">any other documents or information that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_k__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_k__term_1">Municipality</span> may require;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_l" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">proof of payment of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_l__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_l__term_1">application</span> fees;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_m" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-p">a copy of the title deed of the land concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_n" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">a conveyancer’s certificate indicating that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_n__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_n__term_1">application</span> is not restricted by any condition contained in the title deed pertaining to the land concerned or a copy of all historical title deeds; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_o" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_o"><span class="akn-num">(o)</span><span class="akn-p">where applicable, the minutes of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pre_application_consultation" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_o__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_o__term_1">pre-application consultation</span> in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_o__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_o__term_2">application</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_38__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> may at a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pre_application_consultation" id="sec_38__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__term_2">pre-application consultation</span> add or remove any information or documents contemplated in subsection (1) for a particular <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_38__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__term_3">application</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_38__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may issue guidelines regarding the submission of information, documents or procedural requirements.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_39" data-eId="sec_39"><h3>39. Application fees</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_39__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__term_1">applicant</span> must pay the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_39__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> fees determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_39__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__term_3">Municipality</span> before submitting an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_39__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__term_4">application</span> in terms of this By-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Application fees paid to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_39__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> are non-refundable and proof of payment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_39__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> fees must accompany an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_39__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__term_3">application</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_40" data-eId="sec_40"><h3>40. Grounds for refusing to accept <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_40__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__term_1">application</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_41" href="#sec_41">section 41</a>(3) refuse to accept an application if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">there is no proof of payment of the applicable fees; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> is not in the form or does not contain the information or documents referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_38" href="#sec_38">section 38</a>.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_41" data-eId="sec_41"><h3>41. Receipt of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__term_1">application</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commencement" id="sec_41__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__term_2">commencement</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__term_3">application</span> process</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">record receipt of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span>, in writing or by affixing a stamp on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">application</span>, on the day of receipt;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">verify whether the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> complies with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_38" href="#sec_38">section 38</a>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1">applicant</span> in writing within 14 days of receipt of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_2">application</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">application</span> is complete and complies with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_38" href="#sec_38">section 38</a> and that the application process commences; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">of any information, documents or fees referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_38" href="#sec_38">section 38</a> that are outstanding and that the applicant must provide to the Municipality within 14 days of the date of notification.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> must within 14 days of receipt of the outstanding information, documents or fees referred to in subsection (1)(c)(ii) notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_41__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__term_2">applicant</span> in writing that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__term_3">application</span> is complete and that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__term_4">application</span> process commences.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may refuse to consider the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_3__term_2">application</span> if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_41__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_3__term_3">applicant</span> fails to provide the information or documents or pay the fees within the period contemplated in subsection (1)(c)(ii).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> must notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_41__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4__term_2">applicant</span> in writing of a refusal to consider an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4__term_3">application</span> under subsection (3) and must close the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4__term_4">application</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_41__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_5__term_1">applicant</span> has no right of appeal to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_41__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_5__term_2">Appeal Authority</span> in respect of a decision contemplated in subsection (3) to refuse to consider an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_5__term_3">application</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_41__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_6__term_1">applicant</span> wishes to continue with an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_6__term_2">application</span> that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_6__term_3">Municipality</span> refused to consider under subsection (3), the <span class="akn-term"
