data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_41__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_6__term_4">applicant</span> must apply again and pay the applicable <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_6__term_5" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_6__term_5">application</span> fees.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_7__term_1">Municipality</span> must cause notice of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_7__term_2">application</span> to be given within 21 days from the date on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_41__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_7__term_3">application</span> process commences as contemplated in subsection (1)(c)(i) or (2).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_42" data-eId="sec_42"><h3>42. Provision of additional information or documents</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must, within 30 days of receipt of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_42__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> that complies with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_38" href="#sec_38">section 38</a>, notify the applicant in writing of any information or documents it requires in addition to the requirements contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_38" href="#sec_38">section 38</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> must provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span> with the additional information or documents contemplated in subsection (1) within 30 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_3">date of notification</span> or within the further period agreed to between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_4">applicant</span> and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_5">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_42__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3__term_1">applicant</span> fails to provide the additional information or documents within the period contemplated in subsection (2), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span> must consider the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_42__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3__term_3">application</span> without the information or documents and notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_42__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3__term_4">applicant</span> accordingly.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> must, within 21 days of receipt of the additional information or documents, if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_42__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_4__term_2">applicant</span> provided all the required information or documents, acknowledge receipt thereof and notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_42__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_4__term_3">applicant</span> in writing that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_42__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_4__term_4">application</span> process proceeds or that further information, documents or fees are required as a result of the information or documents received.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_5__term_1">Municipality</span> notified the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_42__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_5__term_2">applicant</span> that further information or documents are required as contemplated in subsection (4), subsections (2) and (3) apply to the further submission of information or documents.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_43" data-eId="sec_43"><h3>43. Withdrawal of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_43__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__term_1">application</span> or power of attorney</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_1">applicant</span> may, at any time before the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_2">Municipality</span> makes a decision on an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_3">application</span> submitted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_4">applicant</span>, withdraw the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_5">application</span> by giving written notice of the withdrawal to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_6">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner must in writing inform the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_43__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> if he or she has withdrawn the power of attorney given to his or her former <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_43__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2__term_2">agent</span> and confirm whether he or she will personally proceed with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_43__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2__term_3">application</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_44" data-eId="sec_44"><h3>44. Public notice in accordance with other laws and integrated procedures</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may, on written request and motivation by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">applicant</span>, before notice is given of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">application</span> in terms of section <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">45</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_46" href="#sec_46">46</a>, determine that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a public notice procedure carried out in terms of another law in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> constitutes public notice for the purpose of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">application</span> made in terms of this By-law; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">public notice of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> given in terms of this By-law may be published in accordance with the requirements for public notice applicable to a related <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">application</span> in terms of another law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_44__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> determines that an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_44__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> may be published as contemplated in subsection (1)(b), an agreement must be entered into between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_44__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__term_3">Municipality</span> and the relevant organs of state to facilitate the simultaneous publication of notices.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_45" data-eId="sec_45"><h3>45. Publication of notices</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">section 44</a>, the Municipality must, in accordance with subsection (2), cause public notice to be given of the following applications:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> for a rezoning;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the subdivision of land larger than five hectares inside the outer limit of urban expansion as reflected in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_spatial_development_framework" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipal spatial development framework</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the subdivision of land larger than one hectare outside the outer limit of urban expansion as reflected in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_spatial_development_framework" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipal spatial development framework</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span> has no approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_spatial_development_framework" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">municipal spatial development framework</span>, the subdivision of land larger than five hectares inside the physical edge, including existing urban land use approvals, of the existing urban area;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">Municipality</span> has no approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_spatial_development_framework" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2">municipal spatial development framework</span>, the subdivision of land larger than one hectare outside the physical edge, including existing urban land use approvals, of the existing urban area;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the closure of a public place;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">application</span> in respect of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2">restrictive condition</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">other applications that will materially affect the public interest or the interests of the community if approved.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Public notice of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">application</span> referred to in subsection (1) must be given by—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">publishing a notice with the contents contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_47" href="#sec_47">section 47</a> in newspapers with a general circulation in the area concerned in at least two of the official languages of the Province most spoken in the area concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if there is no newspaper with a general circulation in the area, posting a notice with the contents contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_47" href="#sec_47">section 47</a>, for at least the duration of the notice period, on the land concerned and on any other notice board, as may be determined by the Municipality; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">publishing a notice with the contents contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_47" href="#sec_47">section 47</a> on the Municipality’s website.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_2">applicant</span> to attend to the publication as contemplated in subsection (2) of the public notice of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_3">application</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_45__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_4__term_1">applicant</span> who publishes a notice in terms of this section must within the period determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_4__term_2">Municipality</span> of publication of the notice provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_4__term_3">Municipality</span> with proof, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_4__term_4">Municipality</span>, that the notice was published in accordance with this section.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_46" data-eId="sec_46"><h3>46. Serving of notices</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must cause a notice with the contents contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_47" href="#sec_47">section 47</a> to be served of at least the following applications:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">section 45</a>(1);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a determination of a zoning contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_13" href="#sec_13">section 13</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> for subdivision, amendment or cancellation of a subdivision plan contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(d) and (k) respectively;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">application</span> for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consolidation" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">consolidation</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(e);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the amendment, deletion or imposition of a condition contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(h).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A notice contemplated in subsection (1) must be served—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_35" href="#sec_35">section 35</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in at least two of the official languages of the Province most spoken in the area concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">on each person whose rights or legitimate expectations will be affected by the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">on every owner of land adjoining the land concerned.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may require the serving of a notice as contemplated in this section for any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_46__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__term_2">application</span> made in terms of this By-law and that is not listed in subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_46__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_4__term_2">applicant</span> to attend to the serving of a notice as contemplated in subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_46__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_5__term_1">applicant</span> who serves a notice in terms of this section must within the period determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_5__term_2">Municipality</span> from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_46__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_5__term_3">service</span> of that notice provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_5__term_4">Municipality</span> with proof, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_5__term_5" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_5__term_5">Municipality</span>, of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_46__subsec_5__term_6" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_5__term_6">service</span> of the notice in accordance with subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_46__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_6__term_2">applicant</span> to make the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_46__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_6__term_3">application</span> available for inspection by members of the public at a public place determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_6__term_4">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_47" data-eId="sec_47"><h3>47. Contents of notice</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When notice of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">application</span> must be published or served in terms of this By-law, the notice must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">provide the name and contact details of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">applicant</span> and the owner;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">identify the land or land unit to which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> relates by giving the property description and the physical address;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">state the intent and purpose of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">state that a copy of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">application</span> and supporting documentation will be available for viewing during the hours and at the place mentioned in the notice;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">state the name and contact details of the person to whom <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">comments</span> must be addressed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">invite members of the public to submit written <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">comments</span>, together with the reasons therefor, in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">state in what manner <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">comments</span> may be submitted;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">state the date by which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h__term_1">comments</span> must be submitted, which date may not be less than 30 days from the date on which the notice was given; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">state that any person who cannot write may during office hours come to an address stated in the notice where a named staff member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i__term_1">Municipality</span> will assist those persons by transcribing their <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i__term_2">comments</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_48" data-eId="sec_48"><h3>48. Other methods of public notice</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may cause public notice to be given by one or more of the methods referred to in subsection (2)—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">to ensure additional public notice of applications listed in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">section 45</a>(1) if the Municipality considers notice in accordance with section <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">45</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_46" href="#sec_46">46</a> to be ineffective or expects that the notice would be ineffective; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">to give public notice of any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> in terms of this By-law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Public notice contemplated in subsection (1) may be given by—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">displaying a notice contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_47" href="#sec_47">section 47</a> of a size of at least 60 centimetres by 42 centimetres on the frontage of the erf concerned or at any other conspicuous and easily accessible place on the erf, provided that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the notice is displayed for a minimum of 30 days during any period that the public may comment on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">application</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__term_1">applicant</span>, within 30 days from the last day of display of the notice, submits to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">a sworn affidavit confirming the maintenance of the notice for the prescribed period; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">at least two photos of the notice, one from close up and one from across the street;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">convening a meeting for the purpose of informing affected members of the public of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">broadcasting information regarding the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> on a local radio station in a specified language;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">holding an open day or public meeting to notify and inform affected members of the public of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">publishing the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">application</span> on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_2">Municipality</span>’s website for the duration of the period within which the public may comment on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_3" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_3">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">obtaining letters of consent or objection to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1">application</span>, provided that the letters are accompanied by acceptable evidence that the person signing the letter has been provided with correct and adequate information about the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_2">application</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Additional public notice can be given simultaneously with notice given in accordance with section <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">45</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_46" href="#sec_46">46</a> or thereafter.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_48__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_4__term_2">applicant</span> to attend to the publication of a notice as contemplated in subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_48__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_5__term_1">applicant</span> who gives notice in terms of this section must within the period determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_5__term_2">Municipality</span> of giving notice provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_5__term_3">Municipality</span> with proof, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_5__term_4">Municipality</span> that notice has been given in accordance with subsection (2).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_49" data-eId="sec_49"><h3>49. Requirements for petitions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_49__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Comments in respect of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">application</span> submitted by the public in the form of a petition must clearly state—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the contact details of the authorised representative of the signatories of the petition;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the full name and physical address of each signatory; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">comments</span> and reasons therefor.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_49__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notice to the person contemplated in subsection (1)(a) constitutes notice to all the signatories to the petition.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_50" data-eId="sec_50"><h3>50. Requirements for submission of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_50__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__term_1">comments</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_50__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person may respond to a notice contemplated in section <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">44</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">45</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_46" href="#sec_46">46</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_48" href="#sec_48">48</a> by commenting in writing in accordance with this section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_50__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any comment made as a result of a notice process must be in writing and addressed to the person mentioned in the notice and must be submitted within the period stated in the notice and in the manner set out in this section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_50__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">comments</span> must state the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the name of the person concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the address or contact details at which the person or body concerned will receive notice or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">service</span> of documents;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the interest of the person in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the reason for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1">comments</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_50__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The reasons for any comment must be set out in sufficient detail in order to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">indicate the facts and circumstances that explain the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">comments</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">where relevant demonstrate the undesirable effect the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> will have if approved;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">where relevant demonstrate any aspect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> that is not considered consistent with applicable policy; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">enable the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1">applicant</span> to respond to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_2">comments</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_50__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_50__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_5__term_1">Municipality</span> may refuse to accept <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_50__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_5__term_2">comments</span> submitted after the closing date.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_51" data-eId="sec_51"><h3>51. Intergovernmental participation process</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_51__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to section 45 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_51__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__term_1">Land Use Planning Act</span> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">section 44</a> of this By-law, the Municipality must, simultaneously with the notification to the applicant that an application is complete as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_41" href="#sec_41">section 41</a>(1)(c)(i) or (2) cause notice of the application together with a copy of the application to be given to every municipal department and organ of state that has an interest in the application and request their comment on the application.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_51__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An organ of state must comment on a land use <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">application</span> within 60 days of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">date of notification</span> of a request for comment on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">application</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">receiving all the information necessary to comment if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> is not complete and a request for additional information is made within 14 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">date of notification</span> of the request for comment.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_51__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an organ of state fails to comment within the period referred to in subsection (2), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_51__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> must notify the organ of state’s accounting officer or accounting authority contemplated in the Public Finance Management Act, 1999 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1999/1" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1999/1">Act 1 of 1999</a>), of the failure.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_52" data-eId="sec_52"><h3>52. Amendments before approval</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">applicant</span> may amend his or her <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">application</span> at any time before the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">application</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">applicant</span>’s own initiative;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">as a result of a comment submitted during the notice process; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">at the request of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an amendment to an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_1">application</span> is material, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span> must give notice of the amendment of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_3">application</span> to all municipal departments and other organs of state and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_4">service</span> providers who commented on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_5">application</span> and request them to submit <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_6" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_6">comments</span> on the amended <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_7" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_7">application</span> within 21 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_52__subsec_2__term_8" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__term_8">date of notification</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an amendment to an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_1">application</span> is material, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span> may require that further notice of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_3">application</span> be published or served in terms of section <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">44</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">45</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_46" href="#sec_46">46</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_48" href="#sec_48">48</a>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_53" data-eId="sec_53"><h3>53. Further public notice</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_53__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require that notice of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_53__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> be given again if more than 18 months have elapsed since the first public notice of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_53__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__term_3">application</span> and if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_53__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__term_4">Municipality</span> has not considered the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_53__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__term_5">application</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may, at any stage during the processing of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">application</span> if new information comes to its attention that is material to the consideration of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">application</span>, require—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">notice of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> to be given or served again in terms of section <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">44</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_45" href="#sec_45">45</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_46" href="#sec_46">46</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_48" href="#sec_48">48</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> to be re-sent to municipal departments and, where applicable, other organs of state or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">service</span> providers for comment.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_54" data-eId="sec_54"><h3>54. Liability for cost of notice</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_54__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_54__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_54__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_54__hcontainer_1__term_1">applicant</span> is liable for the costs of publishing and serving of all notices of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_54__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_54__hcontainer_1__term_2">application</span> in terms of this By-law.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_55" data-eId="sec_55"><h3>55. Right of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__term_1">applicant</span> to reply</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Copies of all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_55__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_1__term_1">comments</span> and other information submitted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_55__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_1__term_2">Municipality</span> must be given to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_1__term_3">applicant</span> within 14 days after the closing date for public comment together with a notice informing the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_1__term_4">applicant</span> of his or her rights in terms of this section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> may, within 30 days from the date on which he or she received the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_55__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_2__term_2">comments</span>, submit a written reply thereto to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_55__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_2__term_3">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_3__term_1">applicant</span> may, before the expiry of the period of 30 days referred to in subsection (2), apply to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_55__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span> for an extension of the period to submit a written reply, to an additional period not exceeding 14 days.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_4__term_1">applicant</span> does not submit a reply within the period of 30 days or within an additional period contemplated in subsection (3), if granted, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_4__term_2">applicant</span> is considered to have no comment.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_55__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_5__term_1">Municipality</span> may in writing request additional information or documents from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_5__term_2">applicant</span> as a result of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_55__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_5__term_3">comments</span> received, and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_5__term_4">applicant</span> must supply the information or documents within 30 days of notification of the written request or the further period as may be agreed upon between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_5__term_5" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_5__term_5">applicant</span> and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_55__subsec_5__term_6" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_5__term_6">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_6__term_1">applicant</span> fails to provide the additional information or documents within the period contemplated in subsection (5), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_55__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_6__term_2">Municipality</span> must consider the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_55__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_6__term_3">application</span> without the information or documents and notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_55__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_6__term_4">applicant</span> accordingly.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_56" data-eId="sec_56"><h3>56. Written assessment of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_56__term_1" data-eId="sec_56__term_1">application</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_56__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_56__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> must in writing in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_65" href="#sec_65">section 65</a> assess an application and make a recommendation to the decision-maker regarding the approval or refusal of the application.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_56__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An assessment of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_56__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_2__term_1">application</span> must include a motivation for the recommendation and, where applicable, the proposed conditions of approval.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_57" data-eId="sec_57"><h3>57. Decision-making period</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_57__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> makes a decision in respect of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">application</span> as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_69" href="#sec_69">section 69</a>(1) and no integrated process in terms of another law is being followed, the authorised employee must decide on the application within 60 days, reckoned from—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the last day for the submission of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">comments</span> as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_50" href="#sec_50">section 50</a>(2) if no comments were submitted;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the last day for the submission of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">applicant</span>’s reply to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">comments</span> submitted as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_55" href="#sec_55">section 55</a>(2) or (3); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the last day for the submission of additional information as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_55" href="#sec_55">section 55</a>(5).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_57__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If no integrated process in terms of another law is being followed and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_57__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_2__term_1">Tribunal</span> must decide on an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_57__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_69" href="#sec_69">section 69</a>(2), the Tribunal must decide on the application within 120 days, reckoned from the applicable date contemplated in subsection (1)(a), (b) or (c).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_57__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span>, as the case may be, may extend the period contemplated in subsection (1) or (2) in exceptional circumstances, including the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if an interested person has submitted a petition for intervener status;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span>, if an oral hearing is to be held.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_58" data-eId="sec_58"><h3>58. Failure to act within period</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_58__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_58__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_41" href="#sec_41">section 41</a>(5), an applicant may lodge an appeal with the Appeal Authority if the authorised employee or the Tribunal fails to decide on an application within the period referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_57" href="#sec_57">section 57</a>(1) or (2).</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_59" data-eId="sec_59"><h3>59. Powers to conduct routine inspections</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_59__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> or member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_59__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> may, in accordance with the requirements of this section, enter land or a building to conduct an inspection for the purpose of obtaining information to assess an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_59__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_1__term_3">application</span> in terms of this By-law and to prepare a written assessment contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_56" href="#sec_56">section 56</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When conducting an inspection, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> or member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">request that any record, document or item that is relevant to the purpose of the investigation be produced to assist in the inspection;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">make copies of or take extracts from any document produced by virtue of paragraph (a) that is related to the inspection;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">on providing a receipt, remove a record, document or other item that is related to the inspection;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">inspect any building or structure and make enquiries regarding that building or structure.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may interfere with a person referred to in subsection (1) who is conducting an inspection as contemplated in subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_59__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_4__term_1">authorised employee</span> or member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_59__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_4__term_2">Tribunal</span> must, on request, produce identification showing that he or she is authorised to conduct the inspection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An inspection under subsection (1) must take place at a reasonable time after reasonable notice has been given to the owner, occupier or person in lawful control of the land or building and with the written consent of the owner, occupier or person in lawful control of the land or building.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_60" data-eId="sec_60"><h3>60. Decisions on applications</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An employee authorised by virtue of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_69" href="#sec_69">section 69</a>(1), or the Tribunal by virtue of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_69" href="#sec_69">section 69</a>(2), as the case may be, may in respect of an application contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">approve, in whole or in part, or refuse that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">upon the approval of that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span>, impose conditions in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">conduct any necessary inspection to assess an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_59" href="#sec_59">section 59</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of the <span class="akn-term"
