data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">Tribunal</span>, appoint a technical adviser to advise or assist in the performance of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_60__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">Tribunal</span>’s functions in terms of this By-law.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_61" data-eId="sec_61"><h3>61. Notification and coming into operation of decision</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_61__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must, within 21 days of its decision, in writing notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_61__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__term_2">applicant</span> and any person whose rights are affected by the decision of the decision, the reasons for the decision and their right to appeal, if applicable.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A notice contemplated in subsection (1) must inform an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_61__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> when an approval comes into operation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the owner has appointed an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_61__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_3__term_1">agent</span>, the owner must take steps to ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_61__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_3__term_2">agent</span> notifies him or her of the decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_61__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_3__term_3">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An approval comes into operation only after the expiry of the period contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_79" href="#sec_79">section 79</a>(2) within which an appeal must be lodged if no appeal has been lodged.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to subsection (6), the operation of the approval of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_61__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_5__term_1">application</span> that is the subject of an appeal is suspended pending the decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_61__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_5__term_2">Appeal Authority</span> on the appeal.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an appeal is lodged only against conditions imposed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>, the Tribunal or the authorised employee who imposed the conditions may determine that the approval of the application is not suspended.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_62" data-eId="sec_62"><h3>62. Duties of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_62__term_1" data-eId="sec_62__term_1">agent</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_62__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_62__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_1__term_1">agent</span> must ensure that he or she has the contact details of the owner on whose behalf he or she is authorised to act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_62__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_62__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_2__term_1">agent</span> may not provide information or make a statement in support of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_62__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> which information or statement he or she knows or believes to be misleading, false or inaccurate.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_63" data-eId="sec_63"><h3>63. Errors and omissions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_63__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may at any time correct an error in the wording of its decision if the correction does not change the decision or result in an alteration, insertion, suspension or deletion of a condition of approval.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_63__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> may, on its own initiative or on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_63__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_63__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_2__term_3">applicant</span> or interested party, upon good cause shown, condone an error in a procedure, if the condonation does not have a material adverse effect on, or unreasonably prejudice, any party.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_64" data-eId="sec_64"><h3>64. Exemptions to facilitate expedited procedures</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_64__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may in writing and subject to section 60 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">Land Use Planning Act</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">exempt a development from compliance with a provision of this By­-law to reduce the financial or administrative burden of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">integrated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">application</span> processes contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">section 44</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision of housing with the assistance of a state subsidy; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">incremental upgrading of existing settlements;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">emergency</span> situation authorise that a development may depart from any of the provisions of this By-law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_64__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the Provincial Minister grants an exemption or authorisation to deviate from a provision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_64__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__term_1">Land Use Planning Act</span> to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_64__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span> in terms of section 60 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_64__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__term_3">Land Use Planning Act</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_64__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__term_4">Municipality</span> is exempted from or authorised to deviate from any provision in this By-law that corresponds to the provision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_64__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__term_5">Land Use Planning Act</span> in respect of which an exemption was granted or deviation was authorised.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_V" data-eId="chp_V"><h2>Chapter V<br>Criteria for decision-making</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_65" data-eId="sec_65"><h3>65. General criteria for consideration of applications</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> considers an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">application</span>, it must have regard to the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> submitted in terms of this By-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the procedure followed in processing the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the desirability of the proposed utilisation of land and any guidelines issued by the Provincial Minister regarding the desirability of proposed land uses;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">comments</span> in response to the notice of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">application</span>, including <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">comments</span> received from organs of state, municipal departments and the Provincial Minister in terms of section 45 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_4" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_4">Land Use Planning Act</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the response by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">applicant</span>, if any, to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_2">comments</span> referred to in paragraph (d);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">investigations carried out in terms of other laws that are relevant to the consideration of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">a written assessment by a registered planner appointed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> in respect of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__term_2">application</span> for—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a rezoning;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">a subdivision of more than 20 cadastral units;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a removal, suspension or amendment of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iii__term_1">restrictive condition</span> if it relates to a change of land use;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">an amendment, deletion or imposition of additional conditions in respect of an existing use right;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">an approval of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-overlay_zone" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v__term_1">overlay zone</span> contemplated in the zoning scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">a phasing, amendment or cancellation of a subdivision plan or part thereof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">a closure of a public place or part thereof;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">the impact of the proposed land development on municipal engineering services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the integrated development plan, including the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_spatial_development_framework" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i__term_1">municipal spatial development framework</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">the integrated development plan of the district municipality, including its spatial development framework, where applicable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">the applicable local spatial development frameworks adopted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_k__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_k__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_l" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">the applicable structure plans;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_m" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-p">the applicable policies of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_m__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_m__term_1">Municipality</span> that guide decision­-making;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_n" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">the provincial spatial development framework;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_o" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_o"><span class="akn-num">(o)</span><span class="akn-p">where applicable, a regional spatial development framework contemplated in section 18 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Spatial_Planning_and_Land_Use_Management_Act" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_o__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_o__term_1">Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act</span> and provincial regional spatial development framework;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_p" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_p"><span class="akn-num">(p)</span><span class="akn-p">the policies, principles and the planning and development norms and criteria set by the national and provincial government;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_q" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_q"><span class="akn-num">(q)</span><span class="akn-p">the matters referred to in section 42 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Spatial_Planning_and_Land_Use_Management_Act" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_q__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_q__term_1">Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_r" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_r__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_r__term_1">Land Use Planning Act</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_s" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_s"><span class="akn-num">(s)</span><span class="akn-p">the applicable provisions of the zoning scheme; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_t" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_t"><span class="akn-num">(t)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-restrictive_condition" id="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_t__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_t__term_1">restrictive condition</span> applicable to the land concerned.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_66" data-eId="sec_66"><h3>66. Conditions of approval</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may approve an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_66__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> subject to reasonable conditions that arise from the approval of the proposed utilisation of land.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Conditions imposed in accordance with subsection (1) may include conditions relating to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision of engineering services and infrastructure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">requirements relating to engineering services as contemplated in sections <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_82" href="#sec_82">82</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_83" href="#sec_83">83</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the cession of land or the payment of money;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">settlement restructuring;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">agricultural or heritage resource conservation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">biodiversity conservation and management;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision of housing with the assistance of a state subsidy, social facilities or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-social_infrastructure" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1">social infrastructure</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">energy efficiency;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">requirements aimed at addressing climate change;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">the establishment of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__term_1">owners’ association</span> in respect of the approval of a subdivision;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision of land needed by other organs of state;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_l" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">the endorsement in terms of the Deeds Registries Act in respect of public places where the ownership thereof vests in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_l__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_l__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_m" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_m"><span open space or road as determined in accordance with a policy adopted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_n__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_p"><span class="akn-num">(p)</span><span class="akn-p">the transfer of ownership to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_p__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_p__term_1">Municipality</span> of land needed for other public purposes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_q" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_q"><span class="akn-num">(q)</span><span class="akn-p">the implementation of a subdivision in phases;</span></span><span state;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_s" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_s"><span class="akn-num">(s)</span><span class="akn-p">the submission of a development, including lapsing clauses relating to such phasing;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_v"><span thereto;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_x" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_x"><span class="akn-num">(x)</span><span class="akn-p">the setting of a period within which a particular condition must be met;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y"><span for a temporary departure for a specific occasion or event, which must include—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">parking and the number of ablution facilities required;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the maximum duration or occurrence of the occasional use; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">any other development parameters that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_y__list_1__item_iii__term_1">Municipality</span> may determine;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_z" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__list_1__item_z"><span class="akn-num">(z)</span><span class="akn-p">the payment of a contravention penalty in respect of the unlawful utilisation of land.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> imposes a condition contemplated in subsection (2)(a) or (b), an engineering services agreement must be concluded between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span> and the owner of the land concerned before the construction of engineering services and infrastructure commences on the land.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A condition contemplated in subsection (2)(c) may require only a proportional contribution to municipal public expenditure according to the normal need therefor arising from the approval, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_83" href="#sec_83">section 83</a>(7) and any other applicable provincial norms and standards.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Municipal public expenditure contemplated in subsection (4) includes but is not limited to municipal public expenditure for municipal <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">service</span> infrastructure and amenities relating to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" indoor sports facilities or community halls;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">nature conservation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">energy conservation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">climate change; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">engineering services.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except for land needed for public places or internal engineering services, any additional land required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> or other organs of state arising from an approved subdivision must be acquired subject to the applicable laws that provide for the acquisition or expropriation of land.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_66__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_7__term_1">owners’ association</span> or home <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_66__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_7__term_2">owners’ association</span> that came into being by virtue of a condition imposed under the Land Use Planning Ordinance, 1985 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za-wc013/act/ord/1985/15" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za-wc013/act/ord/1985/15">Ordinance 15 of 1985</a>), and that exists immediately before the commencement of this By-law is regarded as an owners’ association that came into being by virtue of a condition imposed by the Municipality in accordance with this By-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_66__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_8__term_1">Municipality</span> may not approve a land use <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_66__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_8__term_2">application</span> subject to a condition that approval in terms of other legislation is required.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Conditions requiring a standard to be met must specifically refer to an approved or published standard.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No conditions may be imposed that rely on a third party for fulfilment.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Notwithstanding the provisions of any other section in this By-law, a conditional approval of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1__term_1">application</span> lapses if the conditions therein are not complied with within :-</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a period of ten years from the date of such conditional approval, if no period for compliance is specified in such approval; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_11__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the period for compliance specified in such conditional approval, which, together with any extension which may be granted, may not exceed ten years.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_VI" data-eId="chp_VI"><h2>Chapter VI<br>Extension of validity period of approvals</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_67" data-eId="sec_67"><h3>67. Applications for extension of validity period</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_67__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may, on a date before or after the expiry of the validity period of an approval, approve an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_67__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> for the extension of a validity period imposed in terms of a condition of approval if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_67__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__term_3">application</span> for the extension of the period was submitted before the expiry of the validity period.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> considers an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">application</span> in terms of subsection (1), it must have regard to the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">whether the circumstances prevailing at the time of the original approval have materially changed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">whether the legislative or policy requirements applicable to the approval that prevailed at the time of the original approval have materially changed; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">whether there is a pending review <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> in court which may have an effect on the date of implementation of the approval.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If there are material changes in circumstances or in legislative or policy requirements that will necessitate new conditions of approval if an extension of a validity period is approved, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_67__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_3__term_1">application</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(h) must be submitted for consideration before or simultaneously with the application for the extension of a validity period.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The extended validity period takes effect on and is reckoned from the expiry date of the validity period applicable to the original approval or from the expiry date of the previously extended validity period approved in terms of this By-law.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_VII" data-eId="chp_VII"><h2>Chapter VII<br>Municipal planning decision-making structures</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_68" data-eId="sec_68"><h3>68. Municipal planning decision-making structures in respect of applications and appeals</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Applications or appeals are decided—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(a) to (f), (h) to (k), (n), (o) or (r), by an authorised employee who has been authorised by the Municipality to consider and determine the applications as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_69" href="#sec_69">section 69</a>(1);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(a) to (f), (h) to (k), (n), (o) or (r) where an authorised employee has not been authorised by the Municipality to consider and determine the applications as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_69" href="#sec_69">section 69</a>(2), by the Tribunal;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> referred to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(g), (l), (m), (p) or (q), by the Council or an authorised employee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> where an appeal has been lodged against a decision of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">authorised employee</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">Tribunal</span> in respect of applications referred to in paragraph (a) or (b) respectively; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">by the appeal authority referred to in section 62(3) of the Municipal Systems Act where an appeal has been lodged against a decision of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_68__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">authorised employee</span> in respect of applications referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(g), (l), (m), (p) or (q).</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_69" data-eId="sec_69"><h3>69. Consideration of applications</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_69__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_69__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may categorise applications referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(a) to (f), (h) to (k), (n), (o) or (r) for consideration and determination by an. authorised employee.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_69__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_69__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_2__term_1">Tribunal</span> considers and determines all applications referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">section 15</a>(2)(a) to (f), (h) to (k), (n), (o) or (r) that have not been categorised for consideration and determination by an authorised employee.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_70" data-eId="sec_70"><h3>70. Establishment of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_70__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__term_1">Tribunal</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_70__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">establish a Municipal Planning <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">Tribunal</span> for its municipal area;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">by agreement with one or more municipalities establish a joint Municipal Planning <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">agree to the establishment of a district Municipal Planning <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">Tribunal</span> by the district municipality.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_70__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An agreement referred to in subsection (1)(b) or (c) must provide for—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the composition of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the terms and conditions of appointment of members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the determination of rules and procedures at meetings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">Tribunal</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">other matters as may be prescribed in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Spatial_Planning_and_Land_Use_Management_Act" id="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_71" data-eId="sec_71"><h3>71. Composition of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_71__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__term_1">Tribunal</span> for municipal area</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> established in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_70" href="#sec_70">section 70</a>(1)(a) must consist of at least the following members appointed by the Council:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">three employees in the full-time <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">service</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">Municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">two persons who are not employees of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span> or councillors.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_71__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_2__term_1">Tribunal</span> must have knowledge and experience of land use planning or the law related thereto and be representative of a broad range of appropriate experience and expertise.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> appointed in terms of subsection (1)(b) may be—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">an official or employee of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">any department of state or administration in the national or provincial sphere of government;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">a government business enterprise;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a public entity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">organised local government as envisaged in the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">an organisation created by government to provide municipal support;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">a non-governmental organisation; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">any other organ of state not provided for in subparagraphs (i) to (iv); or</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">an individual in his or her own capacity.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_72" data-eId="sec_72"><h3>72. Process for appointment of members for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__term_1">Tribunal</span> for municipal area</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(1)(b) may be appointed by the Council only after the Municipality has—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of an official or employee contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(3)(a), extended a written invitation to nominate an official or employee to serve on the Tribunal to the departments in the national and provincial spheres of government, other organs of state and organisations referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(3)(a); and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of member contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(3)(b), by notice in a newspaper in circulation in the municipal area, invited interested parties to submit, within the period stated in the notice, names of persons who meet the requirements to be so appointed.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An invitation for nominations must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">request sufficient information to enable the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span> to evaluate the knowledge and experience of the nominee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">request a written nomination in the form that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span> determines that complies with subsection (3);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">permit self-nomination; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">provide for a closing date for nominations, which date may not be less than 14 days from the date of publication of the invitation in terms of subsection (1)(b) or the written invitation in terms of subsection (1)(a), and no nominations submitted after that date may be considered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A nomination in response to an invitation must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">provide for acceptance of the nomination by the nominee, if it is not a self-nomination;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">include confirmation by the nominee that he or she is not disqualified from serving as a member in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_74" href="#sec_74">section 74</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">include agreement by the nominee that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">Municipality</span> may verify all the information provided by the nominee; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">include a statement that the nominee will be obliged to commit to and uphold a code of conduct if he or she is appointed.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If no or insufficient nominations are received or if the nominees do not possess the requisite knowledge and experience or comply with any additional criteria which may have been determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__term_2">Municipality</span> must invite nominations for a second time and follow the process required for the invitation for nominations referred to in this section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If after the second invitation for nominations, no or insufficient nominations are received or if the nominees do not possess the requisite knowledge and experience or comply with any additional criteria which may have been determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_5__term_1">Municipality</span>, the executive authority of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_5__term_2">Municipality</span> must designate persons who possess the requisite knowledge and experience and comply with any additional criteria which may have been determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_5__term_3">Municipality</span> and appoint the persons.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Nominations submitted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> by virtue of subsection (1) must be submitted in writing in the form determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_6__term_2">Municipality</span> and must contain the contents referred to in subsection (3).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_7__term_1">Municipality</span> must convene an evaluation panel consisting of officials in the employ of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_7__term_2">Municipality</span> to evaluate nominations that comply with this section as received by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_7__term_3">Municipality</span> and must determine the terms of reference of that evaluation panel.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__term_1">Council</span> must appoint the members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> after having regard to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the recommendations of the evaluation panel;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the knowledge and experience of candidates in respect of land use planning or the law related thereto;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the requirement that the members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_1">Tribunal</span> must be representative of a broad range of appropriate experience and expertise;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the powers and duties of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_d__term_1">Tribunal</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the policy of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_8__list_1__item_e__term_1">Municipality</span> in respect of the promotion of persons previously disadvantaged by unfair discrimination.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__term_1">Council</span> may not appoint a person to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> if that person—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">was not nominated in accordance with the provisions of this section;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is disqualified from appointment as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_74" href="#sec_74">section 74</a>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_9__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">does not possess the knowledge or experience required in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the chairperson of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1">Tribunal</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">another member as deputy chairperson, to act as chairperson of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span> when the chairperson is absent or unable to perform his or her duties.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__term_1">Municipal Manager</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">inform the members in writing of their appointment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">obtain written confirmation from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_1">Council</span> that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_2">Council</span> is satisfied that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_3">Tribunal</span> is in a position to commence its operations; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">after receipt of the confirmation referred to in paragraph (b), publish a notice in the <i>Provincial Gazette</i> of the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the name of each member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the date on which the appointment of each member takes effect;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the term of office of each member; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv__term_1">Tribunal</span> will commence its operation.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_12"><span
