data-eId="sec_72__subsec_12__term_1">Tribunal</span> may commence its operations only after publication of the notice contemplated in subsection (11)(c).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_73" data-eId="sec_73"><h3>73. Term of office and conditions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_73__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__term_1">service</span> of members of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__term_2">Tribunal</span> for municipal area</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A member of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_70" href="#sec_70">section 70</a>(1)(a)—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is appointed for five years or a shorter period as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span> may determine; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">may be appointed for further terms, subject to section 37(1) of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Spatial_Planning_and_Land_Use_Management_Act" id="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The office of a member becomes vacant if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the member is absent from two consecutive meetings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Tribunal</span> without the leave of the chairperson of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the member tenders his or her resignation in writing to the chairperson of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span> or, if the member who is resigning is the chairperson, to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">Council</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the member is removed from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">Tribunal</span> under subsection (3); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the member dies.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Council</span> may, after having given the member an opportunity to be heard, remove a member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">sufficient grounds exist for his or her removal;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the member contravenes the code of conduct referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_76" href="#sec_76">section 76</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the member becomes subject to a disqualification from membership of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">Tribunal</span> as referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_74" href="#sec_74">section 74</a>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A vacancy on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_4__term_1">Tribunal</span> must be filled by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_73__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_4__term_2">Council</span> in terms of section <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">71</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_72" href="#sec_72">72</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A member who is appointed by virtue of subsection (4) holds office for the unexpired part of the period for which the member he or she replaces was appointed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_6__term_1">Tribunal</span> referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(3)(b) must be appointed on the terms and conditions and must be paid the remuneration and allowances and be reimbursed for expenses as determined by the Council.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An official of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> appointed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(1)(a) as a member of the Tribunal—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">may serve as member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1">Tribunal</span> only for as long as he or she is in the full-time employ of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_2">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is bound by the conditions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1">service</span> determined in his or her contract of employment and is not entitled to additional remuneration, allowances, leave or sick leave or any other additional employee benefit as a result of his or her membership on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_2">Tribunal</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A person appointed in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(1)(b) as a member of the Tribunal—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is not an employee on the staff establishment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a person referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(3)(a), is bound by the conditions of service determined in his or her contract of employment and is not entitled to additional remuneration, allowances, leave or sick leave or any other additional employee benefit as a result of his or her membership of the Tribunal;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">performs the specific tasks in respect of the consideration of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> allocated to him or her by the chairperson of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_2">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">sits at such meetings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_d__term_1">Tribunal</span> that requires his or her relevant knowledge and experience as determined by the chairperson of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_d__term_2">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a person referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(3)(b), is entitled to a seating and travel allowance as determined by the Municipality for each meeting of the Tribunal that he or she is required to attend; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_8__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a person referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(3)(b), is not entitled to overtime, annual leave, sick leave, maternity leave, family responsibility leave, study leave, special leave, a performance bonus, medical scheme contribution, pension, motor vehicle or any other benefit to which a municipal employee is entitled to.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The allowances referred to in subsection (8)(e) are subject to taxation in accordance with the normal tax rules that are issued by the South African Revenue Service.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_74" data-eId="sec_74"><h3>74. Disqualification from membership of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_74__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__term_1">Tribunal</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_74__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A person may not be appointed or continue to serve as a member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> if that person—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is not a citizen or permanent resident of the Republic of South Africa;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is a member of Parliament, a Provincial Legislature, a municipal council or a House of Traditional Leaders;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">is an unrehabilitated insolvent;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">has been declared by a court of law to be mentally incompetent or has been detained under the Mental Health Care Act, 2002 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2002/17" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2002/17">Act 17 of 2002</a>);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">has at any time been convicted of an offence involving dishonesty;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">has at any time been removed from an office of trust on account of misconduct;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">has previously been removed from a tribunal for a breach of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Spatial_Planning_and_Land_Use_Management_Act" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act</span> or this By-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">has been found guilty of misconduct, incapacity or incompetence; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">fails to comply with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Spatial_Planning_and_Land_Use_Management_Act" id="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_1">Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act</span> or this By-law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_74__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A member must vacate office if that member becomes subject to a disqualification as contemplated in subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_74__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A member of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">must make full disclosure of any conflict of interest, including any potential conflict; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">may not attend, participate or vote in any proceedings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span> in relation to any matter in respect of which the member has a conflict of interest.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_74__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">For the purposes of this section, a member has a conflict of interest if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the member, a spouse, family member, partner or business associate of the member is the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">applicant</span> or has a pecuniary or other interest in the matter before the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the member has any other interest that may preclude or may reasonably be perceived as precluding the member from performing the functions of the member in a fair, unbiased and proper manner;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the member is an official in the employ of national, provincial or local government, if the department by which such an official is employed has a direct or substantial interest in the outcome of the matter.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_74__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">Council</span> may at any time remove any member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> from office—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if there are reasonable grounds justifying the removal; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">where a member has been disqualified in terms of subsection (1), after giving such a member an opportunity to be heard.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_74__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a member’s appointment is terminated or the member resigns, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_74__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__subsec_6__term_1">Council</span> may appoint a person to fill the vacancy for the unexpired portion of the vacating member’s term of office in accordance with sections <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">71</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_72" href="#sec_72">72</a>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_75" data-eId="sec_75"><h3>75. Meetings of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__term_1">Tribunal</span> for municipal area</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_78" href="#sec_78">section 78</a>, the Tribunal contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_70" href="#sec_70">section 70</a>(1)(a) must determine its own internal arrangements, proceedings and procedures and those of its committees by drafting rules for—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the convening of meetings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the procedure at meetings; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the frequency of meetings.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> may constitute itself to comprise one or more panels to determine—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">applications in specific geographical areas;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">applications in specific areas within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a particular <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> or type or category of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">application</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In this section, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_77" href="#sec_77">section 77</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_78" href="#sec_78">section 78</a>, unless the context indicates otherwise, "the Tribunal" includes a panel of the Tribunal contemplated in subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__term_1">Tribunal</span> must meet at the time and place determined by the chairperson or, in the case of a panel, the presiding officer provided that it must meet at least once per month if there is an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_75__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__term_2">application</span> to consider.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__term_1">Tribunal</span> constitutes itself to comprise a panel, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__term_2">Tribunal</span> must designate at least three members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__term_3">Tribunal</span> to be members of that panel, of whom one must at least be a member contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(1)(b).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A quorum for a meeting of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_6__term_1">Tribunal</span> is the majority of its appointed members.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A quorum for a meeting of a panel of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> is—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the majority of its designated members; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">three members, if the panel consist of only three members.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Meetings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_8__term_1">Tribunal</span> or a panel of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_75__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_8__term_2">Tribunal</span> must be held as contemplated in this section and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_78" href="#sec_78">section 78</a> in accordance with the rules of the Tribunal.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_76" data-eId="sec_76"><h3>76. Code of conduct for members of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_76__term_1" data-eId="sec_76__term_1">Tribunal</span> for municipal area</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_76__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The code of conduct in Schedule 1 applies to every member of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_76__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_76__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a member contravenes the code of conduct, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Council</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of member contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_71" href="#sec_71">section 71</a>(1)(a), institute disciplinary proceedings against the member;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">remove the member from office.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_77" data-eId="sec_77"><h3>77. Administrator for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__term_1">Tribunal</span> for municipal area</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_1">Municipal Manager</span> must appoint or designate an employee as the Administrator and other staff for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_70" href="#sec_70">section 70</a>(1)(a) in terms of the Municipal Systems Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The Administrator must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">liaise with the relevant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Tribunal</span> members and the parties concerned regarding any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">application</span> to be determined by, or other proceedings of, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">maintain a diary of meetings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">allocate a meeting date for, and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">application</span> number to, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">application</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">arrange the attendance of members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">Tribunal</span> at meetings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">arrange venues for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">Tribunal</span> meetings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">perform the administrative functions in connection with the proceedings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that the proceedings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1">Tribunal</span> are conducted efficiently and in accordance with the directions of the chairperson of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_2">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">arrange the affairs of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_h__term_1">Tribunal</span> so as to ensure that time is available to liaise with other organs of state regarding the alignment of integrated applications and authorisations;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">notify the parties concerned of decisions and procedural directives given by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_i__term_1">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">keep a record of all applications submitted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> as well as the outcome of each, including—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">decisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i__term_1">Tribunal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">on-site inspections and any matter recorded as a result thereof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">reasons for decisions; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">proceedings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv__term_1">Tribunal</span>; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">keep records by any means as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_k__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_k__term_1">Tribunal</span> may deem expedient.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_78" data-eId="sec_78"><h3>78. Functioning of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_78__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__term_1">Tribunal</span> for municipal area</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The meetings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_78__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_75" href="#sec_75">section 75</a>(1)(a) must be held at the times and places as the chairperson may determine.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_78__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_2__term_1">applicant</span> or a person whose rights or legitimate expectations will be affected by the approval of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_78__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_2__term_2">application</span> requests to make a verbal representation at a meeting of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_78__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_2__term_3">Tribunal</span>, he or she must submit a written request to the Administrator at least 14 days before that meeting.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Chairperson may approve a request contemplated in subsection (2), subject to reasonable conditions.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">application</span> may be considered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> by means of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the consideration of the written <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">application</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">comments</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">an oral hearing.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_78__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_5__term_1">application</span> may be considered in terms of subsection (4)(a) if it appears to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_78__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_5__term_2">Tribunal</span> that the issues for determination of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_78__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_5__term_3">application</span> can be adequately determined in the absence of the parties by considering the documents or other material lodged with or provided to it.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An oral hearing may be held—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if it appears to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1">Tribunal</span> that the issues for determination of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_2">application</span> cannot be adequately determined in the absence of the parties by considering the documents or other material lodged with or provided to it; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if such hearing would assist in the expeditious and fair disposal of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If appropriate in the circumstances, the oral hearing may be held by electronic means.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_79" data-eId="sec_79"><h3>79. Appeals</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The executive authority is the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_79__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> in respect of decisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_79__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> or an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_79__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__term_3">authorised employee</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_68" href="#sec_68">section 68</a>(a) or (b) and a failure to decide on an application as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_58" href="#sec_58">section 58</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person whose rights are affected by a decision contemplated in subsection (1) may appeal in writing to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_79__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_2__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> within 21 days of notification of the decision.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_79__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__term_1">applicant</span> may appeal in writing to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_79__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__term_2">Appeal Authority</span> in respect of the failure of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_79__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__term_3">Tribunal</span> or an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_79__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__term_4">authorised employee</span> to make a decision within the period contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_57" href="#sec_57">section 57</a>(1), (2) or (3) any time after the expiry of the period contemplated in that section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An appeal is lodged by serving the appeal on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_79__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_4__term_1">Municipal Manager</span> in the form determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_79__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_4__term_2">Municipality</span> and subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_80" href="#sec_80">section 80</a>(1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> considers an appeal, it must have regard to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_65" href="#sec_65">section 65</a>, read with the necessary changes; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1">comments</span> of the Provincial Minister contemplated in section 52 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_2">Land Use Planning Act</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_80" data-eId="sec_80"><h3>80. Procedure for appeal</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An appeal is invalid if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of an appeal contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_79" href="#sec_79">section 79</a>(2), it is not lodged within the period referred to in that subsection; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">it does not comply with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_79" href="#sec_79">sections 79</a>(2) - (4) and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_80" href="#sec_80">80</a>(2) - (7)</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An appeal must set out the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the grounds for the appeal, which may include the following grounds:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">that the administrative action was not procedurally fair as contemplated in the Promotion of Administrative Justice Act, 2000 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/3" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/3">Act 3 of 2000</a>);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">grounds relating to the merits of the land development or land use <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1">application</span> on which the appellant believes the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2">Tribunal</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_3">authorised employee</span> erred in coming to the conclusion that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_4" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_4">Tribunal</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_5" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_5">authorised employee</span> did, as the case may be,</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">whether the appeal is lodged against the whole decision or a part of the decision;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if the appeal is lodged against a part of the decision, a description of the part;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if the appeal is lodged against a condition of approval, a description of the condition;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the factual or legal findings that the appellant relies on;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the relief sought by the appellant;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">any issue that the appellant wishes the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> to consider in making its decision; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_2__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of an appeal in respect of the failure of a decision-maker to make a decision, the facts that prove the failure.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_80__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_3__term_1">applicant</span> who lodges an appeal must within the period referred subsection 79(2), submit proof of payment of appeal fees, as may be determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_80__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span>, to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_3__term_3">Municipal Manager</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_80__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_4__term_1">applicant</span> who lodges an appeal must simultaneously serve notice of the appeal on any person who commented on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_80__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_4__term_2">application</span> concerned and any other person as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_80__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_4__term_3">Municipality</span> may determine.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The notice must be served in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_35" href="#sec_35">section 35</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The notice contemplated in subsection (5) must invite persons to comment on the appeal within 21 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_80__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_6__term_1">date of notification</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The appellant must submit proof of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_80__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_7__term_1">service</span> of the notice as contemplated in subsection (5) to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_7__term_2">Municipal Manager</span> within 14 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_80__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_7__term_3">date of notification</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a person other than the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_80__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_8__term_1">applicant</span> lodges an appeal, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_8__term_2">Municipal Manager</span> must give written notice of the appeal to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_80__subsec_8__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_8__term_3">applicant</span> within 14 days of receipt thereof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_80__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_9__term_1">applicant</span> who has received notice of an appeal in terms of subsection (8) may submit comment on the appeal to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_9__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_9__term_2">Municipal Manager</span> within 21 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_80__subsec_9__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_9__term_3">date of notification</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_80__subsec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_10__term_1">Municipality</span> may refuse to accept any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_80__subsec_10__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_10__term_2">comments</span> on an appeal submitted after the closing date for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_80__subsec_10__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_10__term_3">comments</span> on an appeal.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__term_1">Municipal Manager</span>-</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">may request the Provincial Minister within 14 days of the receipt of an appeal to comment in writing on the appeal within 60 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_a__term_1">date of notification</span> of the request;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">must notify and request the Provincial Minister within 14 days of the receipt of an appeal to comment on the id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a development outside the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">Municipality</span>’s planned outer limit of urban expansion as reflected in its <span class="akn-term" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">Municipality</span> has no approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_spatial_development_framework" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_2">municipal spatial development framework</span>, a development outside the physical edge, including existing urban land use approvals, of the existing urban area;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a rezoning of land zoned for agricultural or conservation purposes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">any category of land use applications as may be prescribed by the Provincial Minister; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">must on receipt of an appeal in terms of this section notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__term_1">applicant</span> in writing whether or not the operation of the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_11__list_1__item_c__term_2">application</span> is suspended.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_12"><span class="akn-num">(12)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> must draft a report assessing an appeal and must submit it to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1__term_2">Municipal Manager</span> within—</span><span class="akn-item" subsections (6) and (9), if no comment was requested in terms of subsection (11); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_12__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">30 days of the closing date for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_13" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_13"><span class="akn-num">(13)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" subsection (12) submit the appeal to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_13__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_13__term_2">Appeal Authority</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_14" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14"><span class="akn-num">(14)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__term_1">Municipal Manager</span> or an employee designated by him or her must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">liaise with the <span class="akn-term" any appeal lodged with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_a__term_2">Appeal Authority</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">maintain a diary of meetings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_b__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">allocate a meeting date for, and appeal number to, an appeal;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">arrange the attendance of members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_d__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> at meetings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">arrange venues for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_e__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">perform the administrative functions in connection with the proceedings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_f__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that the proceedings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_g__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> are conducted efficiently and in accordance with the directions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_g__term_2">Appeal Authority</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">arrange the affairs of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_h__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> so as to ensure that time is available to liaise with other organs of state regarding the alignment of integrated appeal procedures;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">notify the parties concerned of decisions and procedural directives given by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_i__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">keep a record of all appeals lodged as well as the outcome of each, including—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">decisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_i__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">on-site inspections and any matter recorded as a result thereof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">reasons for decisions; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">proceedings of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_j__list_1__item_iv__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">keep records by any means as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_k__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_14__list_1__item_k__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> may deem expedient.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_15" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_15"><span class="akn-num">(15)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An appellant may, at any time before the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_80__subsec_15__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_15__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> makes a decision on an appeal submitted by the appellant, withdraw the appeal by giving written notice of the withdrawal to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_80__subsec_15__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_15__term_2">Municipal Manager</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_16" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_16"><span class="akn-num">(16)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The appellant must in writing inform the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_80__subsec_16__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_16__term_1">Municipality</span> if he or she has withdrawn the power of attorney given to his or her former <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agent" id="sec_80__subsec_16__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_16__term_2">agent</span> and confirm whether he or she will personally proceed with the appeal.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_81" data-eId="sec_81"><h3>81. Consideration by <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An appeal may be considered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> by means of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the consideration of the written appeal and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">comments</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">an oral hearing.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The appeal may be considered in terms of subsection (1)(a) if it appears to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_2__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> that the issues for determination of the appeal can be adequately determined in the absence of the parties by considering the documents or other material lodged with or provided to it.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An oral hearing may be held—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if it appears to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> that the issues for determination of the appeal cannot be adequately determined in the absence of the parties by considering the documents or other material lodged with or provided to it; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if such hearing would assist in the expeditious and fair disposal of the appeal.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If appropriate in the circumstances, the oral hearing may be held by electronic means.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_5__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> decides to hold an oral hearing, any party to the appeal proceedings may appear in person or may be represented by another person.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_6__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> must ensure that every party to a proceeding before the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_6__term_2">Appeal Authority</span> is given an opportunity to present his or her case, whether in writing or orally as contemplated in subsections (2) and (3) and, in particular, to inspect any documents to which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_6__term_3">Appeal Authority</span> proposes to have regard in reaching a decision in the proceeding and to submit <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-comments" id="sec_81__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_6__term_4">comments</span> thereon in accordance with this Chapter or, in the case of an oral hearing, to make submissions in relation to those documents.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">consider and determine all appeals lawfully submitted to it;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">confirm, vary or revoke the decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1">Tribunal</span> or <span
