class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_2">authorised employee</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">provide reasons for any decision made by it;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">give directions relevant to its functions to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">keep a record of all its proceedings; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_7__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">determine whether the appeal falls within its jurisdiction.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to subsection (12), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_8__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> must decide on an appeal within 60 days of receipt of the assessment report as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_80" href="#sec_80">section 80</a>(13).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> revokes a decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__term_2">Tribunal</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__term_3">authorised employee</span> it may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">remit the matter to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Tribunal" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1">Tribunal</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_2">authorised employee</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">if there was an error in the process that was unfair and that cannot be corrected by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">Appeal Authority</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">with instructions regarding the correction of the error; or</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_9__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">replace the decision with any decision it regards necessary.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_10__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> may appoint a technical adviser to advise or assist it with regard to a matter forming part of the appeal.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> must within 21 days from the date of its decision notify the parties to an appeal in writing of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the decision and the reasons therefor; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the decision on an appeal upholds an approval, notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_1">applicant</span> in writing that he or she may act on the approval.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_12"><span class="akn-num">(12)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Appeal_Authority" id="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1__term_1">Appeal Authority</span> may extend the period contemplated in subsection (8) in exceptional circumstances, including the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if an interested person has submitted a petition for intervener status;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_12__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if an oral hearing is to be held.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_VIII" data-eId="chp_VIII"><h2>Chapter VIII<br>Provision of engineering services</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_82" data-eId="sec_82"><h3>82. Responsibility for provision of engineering services</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_82__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_82__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_1__term_1">applicant</span> is responsible for the provision, installation and costs of internal engineering services required for a development once an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_82__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> is approved.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_82__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_82__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> is responsible for the provision and installation of external engineering services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_82__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_82__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> is not the provider of an engineering <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_82__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_3__term_2">service</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_82__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_3__term_3">applicant</span> must satisfy the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_82__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_3__term_4">Municipality</span> that adequate arrangements have been made with the relevant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_82__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_3__term_5">service</span> provider for the provision of that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_82__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_3__term_6">service</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_82__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may enter into a written agreement with an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__term_2">applicant</span> to provide that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">applicant</span> is responsible for the provision, installation and costs of external engineering services instead of paying the applicable development charges; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">applicant</span> is responsible for the provision, installation and costs of external engineering services and that the fair and reasonable costs of the external engineering services may be set off against the development charges payable by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_82__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2">applicant</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_83" data-eId="sec_83"><h3>83. Development charges and other contributions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_83__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_83__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_1__term_1">applicant</span> must pay development charges to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_83__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_1__term_2">Municipality</span> in respect of the provision and installation of external engineering services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_83__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">These external engineering services for which development charges are payable must be set out in a policy adopted and annually reviewed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_83__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_83__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The amount of the development charges payable by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_83__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_3__term_1">applicant</span> must be calculated in accordance with the policy adopted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_83__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_83__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The date by which development charges must be paid and the means of payment must be specified in the conditions of approval.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_83__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The development charges imposed are subject to escalation at the rate calculated in accordance with the policy on development charges.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_83__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_83__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> must annually submit a report to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Council" id="sec_83__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_6__term_2">Council</span> on the development charges paid to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_83__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_6__term_3">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_83__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When determining the contribution contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>(4) and (5), the Municipality must have regard to provincial norms and standards as well as—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the municipal <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1">service</span> infrastructure and amenities for the land concerned that are needed for the approved land use;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the public expenditure on that infrastructure and those amenities incurred in the past and that facilitates the approved land use;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the public expenditure on that infrastructure and those amenities that may arise from the approved land use;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">money in respect of contributions contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>(4) paid in the past by the owner of the land concerned; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_83__subsec_7__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">money in respect of contributions contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>(4) to be paid in the future by the owner of the land concerned.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_84" data-eId="sec_84"><h3>84. Land for parks, open spaces and other uses</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_84__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> approves an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_84__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__term_2">application</span> for the use of land for residential purposes, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_84__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__term_3">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_84__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__term_4">applicant</span> to provide land for parks or public open spaces in terms of conditions of approval imposed in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The extent of land required for parks or public open spaces is determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_84__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> in accordance with a policy adopted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_84__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The land required for parks or public open spaces must be provided within the land area of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_84__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_3__term_1">application</span> or may, with the consent of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_84__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_3__term_2">Municipality</span>, be provided elsewhere within the municipal area.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_84__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_4__term_1">application</span> is approved without the required provision of land for parks or open spaces within the land area of the development, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_84__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_4__term_2">applicant</span> may be required to pay money to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_84__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_4__term_3">Municipality</span> in lieu of the provision of land.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_IX" data-eId="chp_IX"><h2>Chapter IX<br>Enforcement</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_85" data-eId="sec_85"><h3>85. Enforcement</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_85__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must comply and enforce compliance with—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the provisions of this By-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the provisions of a zoning scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">conditions imposed in terms of this By-law or any law repealed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">Land Use Planning Act</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_85__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_85__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> may not do anything that is in conflict with subsection (1).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_86" data-eId="sec_86"><h3>86. Offences and penalties</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_86__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A person is guilty of an offence and is liable on conviction to a fine or imprisonment not exceeding 20 years or to both a fine and such imprisonment if he or she—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">contravenes or fails to comply with sections <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_15" href="#sec_15">15</a>(1) and (4), <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_20" href="#sec_20">20</a>(1), <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_21" href="#sec_21">21</a>(4), <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_31" href="#sec_31">31</a>(1), <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_59" href="#sec_59">59</a>(3), <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_62" href="#sec_62">62</a>(2) or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_88" href="#sec_88">88</a>(2);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">utilises land in a manner other than prescribed by a zoning scheme without the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">upon registration of the transfer of ownership of the first land unit arising from a subdivision to a person other than the developer, fails to transfer all common property arising from the subdivision to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owners__association" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">owners’ association</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">supplies particulars, information or answers in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">application</span>, or in an appeal against a decision on an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">application</span>, or in any documentation or representation related to an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">application</span> or an appeal, knowing it to be false, incorrect or misleading or not believing them to be correct;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">falsely professes to be an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">authorised employee</span> or the interpreter or assistant of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2">authorised employee</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">hinders or interferes with an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">authorised employee</span> in the exercise of any power or the performance of any duty of that employee.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_86__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An owner who permits his or her land to be used in a manner set out in subsection (1)(b) and who does not cease that use or take reasonable steps to ensure that the use ceases, is guilty of an offence and liable upon conviction to a fine or imprisonment not exceeding 20 years or to both a fine and such imprisonment.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_86__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person convicted of an offence in terms of this By-law who, after conviction, continues with the action in respect of which he or she was so convicted, is guilty of a continuing offence and liable upon conviction to imprisonment for a period not exceeding three months or to an equivalent fine or to both such fine and imprisonment, in respect of each day on which he or she so continues or has continued with that act or omission.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_86__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_86__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-adopt" id="sec_86__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_4__term_2">adopt</span> fines and contravention penalties to be imposed in the enforcement of this By-law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_87" data-eId="sec_87"><h3>87. Serving of compliance notices</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_87__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must serve a compliance notice on a person if it has reasonable grounds to suspect that the person is guilty of an offence in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_86" href="#sec_86">section 86</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A compliance notice must instruct the person to cease the unlawful utilisation of land or construction activity or both, without delay or within the period determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span>, and may include an instruction to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">demolish, remove or alter any building, structure or work unlawfully erected or constructed or to rehabilitate the land or restore the building concerned to its original form or to cease the activity, as the case may be, within the period determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Manager" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipal Manager</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">submit an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">application</span> for the approval of the utilisation of the land or construction activity in terms of this By-law within 30 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">service</span> of the compliance notice and to pay the contravention penalty within 30 days of the approval of the utilisation; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">rectify the contravention of or non-compliance with a condition of approval within a specified period.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person who has received a compliance notice with an instruction contemplated in subsection (2)(a) may not submit an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_87__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_3__term_1">application</span> in terms of subsection (2)(b).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An instruction to submit an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_87__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_4__term_1">application</span> in terms of subsection (2)(b) must not be construed as an indication that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_87__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_4__term_2">application</span> will be approved.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_87__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_5__term_1">application</span> submitted in terms of subsection (2)(b) is refused, the owner must demolish, remove or alter the building, structure or work unlawfully erected or constructed and rehabilitate the land or restore the building.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person who received a compliance notice in terms of this section may object to the notice by submitting written representations to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_87__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> within 30 days of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-date_of_notification" id="sec_87__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_6__term_2">date of notification</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_88" data-eId="sec_88"><h3>88. Contents of compliance notice</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A compliance notice must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">identify the person to whom it is addressed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">describe the alleged unlawful utilisation of land or construction activity and the land on which it is occurring or has occurred;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">state that the utilisation of land or construction activity is unlawful and inform the person of the particular offence contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_86" href="#sec_86">section 86</a> which that person allegedly has committed or is committing by the continuation of that activity on the land;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">state the steps that the person must take and the period within which those steps must be taken;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">state anything which the person may not do and the period during which the person may not do it;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">make provision for the person to submit representations in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_89" href="#sec_89">section 89</a> with the contact person stated in the notice; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">issue a warning to the effect that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the person may be prosecuted for and convicted of an offence contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_86" href="#sec_86">section 86</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">on conviction of an offence, the person will be liable for the penalty as provided for;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the person may be required by an order of court to demolish, remove or alter any building, structure or work unlawfully erected or constructed or to rehabilitate the land or restore the building concerned or to cease the activity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a contravention relating to a consent use or temporary departure, the approval may be withdrawn; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v__term_1">application</span> for authorisation of the activity or development parameter, the contravention penalty in the amount as stated in the notice, including any costs incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v__term_2" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_v__term_2">Municipality</span>, may be imposed.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person on whom a compliance notice is served must comply with that notice within the period stated in the notice unless the person has objected to the notice in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_89" href="#sec_89">section 89</a> and the Municipality has not decided on the matter in terms of that section or the Municipality has agreed to suspend the operation of the compliance notice in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_89" href="#sec_89">section 89</a>(2).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_89" data-eId="sec_89"><h3>89. Objections to compliance notice</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who receives a compliance notice in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_87" href="#sec_87">section 87</a> may object to the notice by making written representations to the Municipality within 30 days of the date of notification.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">After consideration of any objections or representations made in terms of subsection (1) and any other relevant information, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">may suspend, confirm, vary or withdraw the compliance notice or any part of the compliance notice; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">must specify the period within which the person to whom the compliance notice is addressed must comply with any part of the compliance notice that is confirmed or varied.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_90" data-eId="sec_90"><h3>90. Failure to comply with compliance notice</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a person fails to comply with a compliance notice, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">lay a criminal charge against the person;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">apply to the court for an order—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">restraining that person from continuing the unlawful utilisation of the land;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">directing that person to, without the payment of compensation—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">demolish, remove or alter any building, structure or work unlawfully erected or constructed; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">rehabilitate the land concerned;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_90__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a consent use or temporary departure, withdraw the approval granted and take any of the other steps contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_88" href="#sec_88">section 88</a>(1)(g).</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_91" data-eId="sec_91"><h3>91. Compliance certificates</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_91__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> who is satisfied that the owner or occupier of any land or premises has complied with a compliance notice may issue a certificate, in the manner and form determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1__term_2">Municipality</span>, to confirm the compliance.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_91__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_2__term_1">authorised employee</span> must submit a report to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span> regarding his or her findings contemplated in subsection (1) and the issuing of a compliance certificate.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_92" data-eId="sec_92"><h3>92. Urgent matters</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_92__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> does not have to comply with sections <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_87" href="#sec_87">87</a>(6), <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_88" href="#sec_88">88</a>(1)(f) and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_89" href="#sec_89">89</a> in a case where an unlawful utilisation of land must be stopped urgently and may issue a compliance notice calling upon the person or owner to cease the unlawful utilisation of land immediately.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the person or owner fails to cease the unlawful utilisation of land immediately, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_92__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> may apply to the court for an urgent interdict or any other relief necessary.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_93" data-eId="sec_93"><h3>93. General powers and functions of authorised employees</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_93__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_93__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> may, with the written consent of the owner, occupier or person in lawful control of the land or building without a warrant and after reasonable notice has been given to the owner, occupier or person in lawful control of the land or building, enter upon land or premises or enter a building at any reasonable time for the purpose of ensuring compliance with this By-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_93__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_93__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_2__term_1">authorised employee</span> must be in possession of proof that he or she has been designated as an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_93__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_2__term_2">authorised employee</span> for the purposes of subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_93__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_93__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_3__term_1">authorised employee</span> may be accompanied by an interpreter, a police official or any other person who may be able to assist with the inspection.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_94" data-eId="sec_94"><h3>94. Powers of entry, search and seizure</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_94__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In ensuring compliance with this By-law an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">authorised employee</span> may in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_93" href="#sec_93">section 93</a>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">question any person on land or premises entered upon or in a building entered who, in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">authorised employee</span>, may be able to provide information on a matter that relates to an investigation regarding an offence in terms of, or contravention of, this By-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">question any person on that land or those premises or in that building about any act or omission in respect of which there is a reasonable suspicion that it constitutes—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">an offence in terms of this By-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">a contravention of this By-law; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a contravention of an approval or a term or condition of that approval;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">question that person about any structure, object, document, book, record, written or electronic information or inspect any structure, object, document, book, record or written or electronic information that may be relevant for the purpose of the investigation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">copy or make extracts from any document, book, record, written or electronic information referred to in paragraph (c), or remove that document, book, record or written or electronic information in order to make copies thereof or extracts therefrom;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">require that person to produce or deliver to a place specified by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">authorised employee</span> any document, book, record, written or electronic information referred to in paragraph (c) for inspection;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">examine that document, book, record, written or electronic information or make a copy thereof or an extract therefrom;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">require from that person an explanation of any entry in that document, book, record, written or electronic information;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">inspect any article, substance, plant or machinery which is or was on the land, or any work performed on the land or any condition prevalent on the land, or remove for examination or analysis any article, substance, plant or machinery or a part or sample thereof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">take photographs or make audio-visual recordings of anything or any person on that land or those premises or in that building relevant to the purposes of the investigation; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">seize a book, record, written or electronic information referred to in paragraph (c) or article, substance, plant or machinery referred to in paragraph (h) or a part or sample thereof that in his or her opinion may serve as evidence at the trial of the person to be charged with an offence under this By-law or the common law, provided that the user of the article, substance, plant or machinery on the land or premises or in the building concerned may make copies of that book, record or document before the seizure.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_94__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_94__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__term_1">authorised employee</span> removes or seizes any article, substance, plant or machinery, book, record or other document as contemplated in this section, he or she must issue a receipt to the owner or person in control thereof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_94__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_94__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_3__term_1">authorised employee</span> may not have a direct or indirect personal or private interest in the matter to be investigated.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_95" data-eId="sec_95"><h3>95. Warrant of entry for enforcement purposes</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A judge of a High Court or a Magistrate for the district in which the land is situated may, at the request of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span>, issue a warrant to enter upon the land or premises or building if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the prior permission of the occupier or owner cannot be obtained after reasonable attempts; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the purpose of the inspection would be frustrated by the occupier or owner’s prior knowledge thereof.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A warrant may be issued only if it appears to the Judge or Magistrate from information on oath or affirmation that there are reasonable grounds for believing that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">authorised employee</span> has been refused entry to land or a building that he or she is entitled to inspect;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_employee" id="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">authorised employee</span> will be refused entry to land or a building that he or she is entitled to inspect;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">an offence contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_86" href="#sec_86">section 86</a> is occurring or has occurred and an inspection of the premises is likely to yield information pertaining to that offence; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the inspection is reasonably necessary for the purposes of this By­-law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A warrant must authorise the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> to enter upon the land or premises or to enter the building to take any of the measures referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_94" href="#sec_94">section 94</a> as specified in the warrant, on one occasion only, and that entry must occur—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">within one month of the date on which the warrant was issued; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">at a reasonable time, except where the warrant was issued on grounds of urgency.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_96" data-eId="sec_96"><h3>96. Regard to decency and order</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_96__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_96__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The entry upon land or premises or in a building under this Chapter must be conducted with strict regard to decency and order, which must include regard to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a person’s right to respect for and protection of his or her dignity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the right to freedom and security of the person; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_96__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a person’s right to personal privacy.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_97" data-eId="sec_97"><h3>97. Enforcement litigation</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_97__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_97__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Whether or not the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> lays criminal charges against a person for an offence contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_86" href="#sec_86">section 86</a>, and despite <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_87" href="#sec_87">section 87</a>, the Municipality may apply to the court for an interdict or any other appropriate order, including an order compelling that person to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">demolish, remove or alter any building, structure or work unlawfully erected or constructed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">rehabilitate the land concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_97__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">cease the unlawful utilisation of land.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_X" data-eId="chp_X"><h2>Chapter X<br>Miscellaneous</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_98" data-eId="sec_98"><h3>98. Naming and numbering of streets</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If as a result of the approval of a development <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_98__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1__term_1">application</span> streets or roads are created, whether public or private, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_98__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1__term_2">Municipality</span> must approve the naming of streets and must allocate a street number to each of the erven or land units located in such street or road.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The proposed names of the streets and numbers must be submitted as part of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_98__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_2__term_1">application</span> for subdivision.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In considering the naming of streets, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_98__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> must take into account the relevant policies regarding street naming and numbering.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_98__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> must notify the Surveyor-General of the approval of new streets as a result of the approval of an amendment or cancellation of a subdivision plan in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_23" href="#sec_23">section 23</a> and the Surveyor-General must endorse the records of the Surveyor-General’s Office to reflect the amendment or cancellation of the street names on an approved general plan.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_99" data-eId="sec_99"><h3>99. Repeal and transitional arrangements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_99__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The by-law listed in Schedule 2 is repealed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_99__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any action taken, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-application" id="sec_99__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_2__term_1">application</span> or appeal lodged in terms of the By-law listed in Schedule 2 and that has not been finalised before this by-law comes into operation, must be administered and finalised as if the By-law listed in Schedule 2, had not been repealed.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_100" data-eId="sec_100"><h3>100. Short title and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commencement" id="sec_100__term_1" data-eId="sec_100__term_1">commencement</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_100__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This By-law is called the Bergrivier <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_100__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> By-law on Municipal Land Use Planning 2020.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_100__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This By-law comes into operation on the date it is published in the <i>Provincial Gazette</i>.</span></span></section></section></section></span><span class="akn-attachments"><div class="akn-attachment" id="att_1" data-eId="att_1">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 1</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Code of conduct for members of Tribunal</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="att_1/hcontainer_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1">General conduct</h3>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_1/para_1" data-eId="para_1"><span class="akn-num">1.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_1/para_1__list_1" data-eId="para_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A member of the Tribunal must at all times—</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">act in accordance with the principles of accountability and transparency; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">disclose his or her personal interests in any decision to be made in the planning process in which he or she serves or has been requested to serve;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">abstain completely from direct or indirect participation as an advisor in any matter in which he or she has a personal interest and leave any chamber in which such matter is under deliberation unless the personal interest has been made a matter of public record and the Council has given written approval and has expressly authorised his or her participation.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_1/para_2" data-eId="para_2"><span class="akn-num">2.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_1/para_2__list_1" data-eId="para_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A member of the Tribunal may not—</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="para_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">use his or her position or privileges as Tribunal member or confidential information obtained as a Tribunal member, for private gain or to improperly benefit another person; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="para_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">participate as a decision-maker concerning a matter in which that Tribunal member or that member’s spouse, family member, partner or business associate has a direct or indirect personal interest or private business interest.</span></span></span></span></span><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="att_1/hcontainer_2" data-eId="hcontainer_2">Gifts</h3>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_1/para_3" data-eId="para_3"><span class="akn-num">3.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A member of the Tribunal may not receive or seek gifts, favours or any other offer under circumstances in which it might reasonably be inferred that the gifts, favours or offers are intended or expected to influence that member’s objectivity as an advisor or decision-maker in the planning process.</span></span></span><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="att_1/hcontainer_3" data-eId="hcontainer_3">Undue influence</h3>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_1/para_4" data-eId="para_4"><span class="akn-num">4.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_1/para_4__list_1" data-eId="para_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A member of the Tribunal may not—</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="para_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">use the power of his or her office to seek or obtain special advantage for private gain or to improperly benefit another person that is not in the public interest;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="para_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">use confidential information acquired in the course of his or her duties to further a personal interest;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="para_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">disclose confidential information acquired in the course of his or her duties unless required by law to do so or by circumstances to prevent substantial prejudice or damage to another person; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/para_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="para_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">commit a deliberately wrongful act that reflects adversely on the Tribunal, the Municipality, the government or the planning profession by seeking business by stating or implying that he or she is prepared, willing or able to influence decisions of the Tribunal by improper means.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>
</div>
<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_2" data-eId="att_2">

<h2 class="akn-subheading">By-law repealed by section 99</h2>

</div></span></article></span>
